Rest Architecture

<a href="https://www.gitbook.com/?utm_source=content&amp;utm_medium=trademark&amp;utm_campaign=-MkP23pBP3MWkIzJcreW" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1uwl36a r-z2wwpe r-1rasi3h r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz r-1fdo3w0 r-1mnahxq r-ymttw5 r-5njf8e r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgNTEyIDUxMiIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItZXUza2Egci0xYW9ja2lkIiBzdHlsZT0idmVydGljYWwtYWxpZ246bWlkZGxlIj48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTIzMC40MzQgMzc5LjU1NGM4LjI1OSAwIDE0Ljk3OCA2LjcxOSAxNC45NzggMTQuOTc0IDAgOC4yNTYtNi43MTkgMTQuOTc0LTE0Ljk3OCAxNC45NzQtOC4yNTUgMC0xNC45NzQtNi43MTgtMTQuOTc0LTE0Ljk3NCAwLTguMjU1IDYuNzE5LTE0Ljk3NCAxNC45NzQtMTQuOTc0em0yMzUuMTg5LTkyLjc1OGMtOC4yNTkgMC0xNC45NzgtNi43MTktMTQuOTc4LTE0Ljk3NCAwLTguMjU5IDYuNzE5LTE0Ljk3OCAxNC45NzgtMTQuOTc4IDguMjU1IDAgMTQuOTc0IDYuNzE5IDE0Ljk3NCAxNC45NzggMCA4LjI1NS02LjcxOSAxNC45NzQtMTQuOTc0IDE0Ljk3NHptMC02MS4zNTFjLTI1LjU3MSAwLTQ2LjM3NyAyMC44MDUtNDYuMzc3IDQ2LjM3NyAwIDQuOTc5LjgyNyA5LjkzOCAyLjQ2IDE0Ljc1N0wyNjguNTAyIDM2OC4xM2MtOC43MDQtMTIuNTQzLTIyLjgxMi0xOS45NzktMzguMDY4LTE5Ljk3OS0xNy42NzYgMC0zMy43OTEgMTAuMTEzLTQxLjU4NiAyNS45MjRMNTEuMjExIDMwMS41MTRjLTE0LjU0LTcuNjQ2LTI1LjQyNS0zMS41OTUtMjQuMjctNTMuMzkyLjU5OC0xMS4zNzEgNC41My0yMC4xOTYgMTAuNTExLTIzLjYwNCAzLjgtMi4xNTcgOC4zNy0xLjk2OCAxMy4yMTQuNTdsLjkyLjQ4NWMzNi40NjQgMTkuMjEyIDE1NS44MjIgODIuMDc5IDE2MC44NDQgODQuNDEzIDcuNzU3IDMuNTg2IDEyLjA2OSA1LjA0MSAyNS4yNzktMS4yMjJsMjQ2LjcyMy0xMjguMzE3YzMuNjE1LTEuMzY1IDcuODMyLTQuODMgNy44MzItMTAuMDkxIDAtNy4zLTcuNTQ2LTEwLjE3Ny03LjU2OC0xMC4xNzctMTQuMDI2LTYuNzI5LTM1LjYwMS0xNi44MjctNTYuNjM5LTI2LjY3Ni00NC45NjUtMjEuMDU1LTk1LjkzMy00NC45MTktMTE4LjMxOC01Ni42MzktMTkuMzIzLTEwLjExNi0zNC44NzctMS41OS0zNy42NS4xMzVsLTUuMzkgMi42NjdDMTY1Ljk2NSAxMjkuNDgyIDMxLjE1NCAxOTYuMjQ4IDIzLjQ3OSAyMDAuOTE3IDkuNzM1IDIwOS4yOCAxLjIyNCAyMjUuOTQuMTIyIDI0Ni42MjVjLTEuNzIyIDMyLjc4OSAxNS4wMDcgNjYuOTY5IDM4LjkxNiA3OS41MTJsMTQ1LjUzNiA3NS4wNTdjMy4yNzkgMjIuNzA5IDIyLjgyNyAzOS43MTIgNDUuODYgMzkuNzEyIDI1LjMzNyAwIDQ1Ljk5Mi0yMC40MjUgNDYuMzc0LTQ1LjY3MmwxNjAuMjkyLTg2Ljg3YTQ2LjQxIDQ2LjQxIDAgMDAyOC41MjMgOS44MzVjMjUuNTcxIDAgNDYuMzc3LTIwLjgwNiA0Ni4zNzctNDYuMzc3IDAtMjUuNTcyLTIwLjgwNi00Ni4zNzctNDYuMzc3LTQ2LjM3N3oiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" Accessibility

# 

<span key="71a2edd734c542bd8b3698896c6baeb0"><span offset-key="71a2edd734c542bd8b3698896c6baeb0:0">So what is accessibility?</span></span>

<span key="8065a70cb6e147f099a20e39a67abd17"><span offset-key="8065a70cb6e147f099a20e39a67abd17:0">Accessibility is the practice of making your websites usable by as many people as possible. We traditionally think of this as being about people with disabilities, but the practice of making sites accessible also benefits other groups such as those using mobile devices, or those with slow network connections.</span></span>

<span key="7e7657c4de3a40e4b00405e5ac12ad97"><span offset-key="7e7657c4de3a40e4b00405e5ac12ad97:0">You might also think of accessibility as treating everyone the same, and giving them equal opportunities, no matter what their ability or circumstances. Just as it is wrong to exclude someone from a physical building because they are in a wheelchair (modern public buildings generally have wheelchair ramps or elevators), it is also not right to exclude someone from a website because they have a visual impairment. We are all different, but we are all human, and therefore have the same human rights.</span></span>

<span key="5ef45b8e797e40d89355debc68f9efb6"><span offset-key="5ef45b8e797e40d89355debc68f9efb6:0">Accessibility is the right thing to do. Providing accessible sites is part of the law in some countries, which can open up some significant markets that otherwise would not be able to use your services or buy your products.</span></span>

<span key="08c220ac557f4dfc888e45689f2ef26d"><span offset-key="08c220ac557f4dfc888e45689f2ef26d:0">Building accessible sites benefit everyone:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="060581d0708f45eb91310c03bb5ccc35"><span offset-key="060581d0708f45eb91310c03bb5ccc35:0">Semantic HTML, which improves accessibility, also improves SEO, making your site more findable.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="7425a5c91d1442bea48691600a486f55"><span offset-key="7425a5c91d1442bea48691600a486f55:0">Caring about accessibility demonstrates good ethics and morals, which improves your public image.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="fc65da00e1cc4f92bb10040729860894"><span offset-key="fc65da00e1cc4f92bb10040729860894:0">Other good practices that improve accessibility also make your site more usable by other groups, such as mobile phone users or those on low network speed. In fact, everyone can benefit from many such improvements.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="1f6b1f54367c48408f1563c7ab432d6f"><span offset-key="1f6b1f54367c48408f1563c7ab432d6f:0">Did we mention it is also the law in some places?</span></span>

## 

<span key="9ae0c8f5917b408da0d7ba908997dcbb"><span offset-key="9ae0c8f5917b408da0d7ba908997dcbb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#what_kinds_of_disability_are_we_looking_at" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fd0a365f6da54c738b1fbbf8559efec4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a455d96607a64802b8e2fff0d5777e25"><span data-offset-key="a455d96607a64802b8e2fff0d5777e25:0">What kinds of disability are we looking at?</span></span></span></a><span key="1dd9a8c6a88f4b038b26b29b2e2f0a14"><span offset-key="1dd9a8c6a88f4b038b26b29b2e2f0a14:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="bd784378abb946959b9ebc6e5ac5ec70"><span offset-key="bd784378abb946959b9ebc6e5ac5ec70:0">People with disabilities are just as diverse as people without disabilities, and so are their disabilities. The key lesson here is to think beyond your own computer and how you use the web, and start learning about how others use it â€” </span>*you are not your users*<span offset-key="bd784378abb946959b9ebc6e5ac5ec70:2">. The main types of disability to consider are explained below, along with any special tools they use to access web content (known as </span>**assistive technologies**<span offset-key="bd784378abb946959b9ebc6e5ac5ec70:4">, or </span>**ATs**<span offset-key="bd784378abb946959b9ebc6e5ac5ec70:6">).</span></span>

<span key="e34bbd4b39a64f2ca4e6e7ae05f3aae4">**Note:**<span offset-key="e34bbd4b39a64f2ca4e6e7ae05f3aae4:1"> The World Health Organization's </span></span><a href="https://www.who.int/en/news-room/fact-sheets/detail/disability-and-health" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ad0ffa3c41944e34a8b11f7ca307f48d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="6c1538e9ce1f4d6791dc0b30a7b01ec2"><span data-offset-key="6c1538e9ce1f4d6791dc0b30a7b01ec2:0">Disability and health</span></span></span></a><span key="bb7626b5ff4446e0819221946b9120f7"><span offset-key="bb7626b5ff4446e0819221946b9120f7:0"> fact sheet states that "Over a billion people, about 15% of the world's population, have some form of disability", and "Between 110 million and 190 million adults have significant difficulties in functioning."</span></span>

### 

<span key="2cd812b51d22493e9e3f62816fe96807"><span offset-key="2cd812b51d22493e9e3f62816fe96807:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#people_with_visual_impairments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1952b4ce74224b37a881d887dce7f47a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b1d4f5d09a6f485eab55460d84a8fe55"><span data-offset-key="b1d4f5d09a6f485eab55460d84a8fe55:0">People with visual impairments</span></span></span></a><span key="6e53b79a32dd4e96a28c83e98730e183"><span offset-key="6e53b79a32dd4e96a28c83e98730e183:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="53db90b399b840b098041472f33c302a"><span offset-key="53db90b399b840b098041472f33c302a:0">People with visual impairments include people with blindness, low-level vision, and color blindness. Many people with visual impairments use screen magnifiers that are either physical magnifiers or software zoom capabilities. Most browsers and operating systems these days have zoom capabilities. Some users will rely on screen readers, which is software that reads digital text aloud. Some screen reader examples include:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="c8e02e57bdcc437ab197b9b9039343ce"><span offset-key="c8e02e57bdcc437ab197b9b9039343ce:0">Paid commercial products, like </span></span><a href="https://www.freedomscientific.com/Products/software/JAWS/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="364bc68f04984a038c60db625d1fcc6f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c9b3d105df634ce7bdd1c14acb45bc47"><span data-offset-key="c9b3d105df634ce7bdd1c14acb45bc47:0">JAWS</span></span></span></a><span key="205fc2d148ae404b85185305a7488c53"><span offset-key="205fc2d148ae404b85185305a7488c53:0"> (Windows) and </span></span><a href="https://yourdolphin.com/screenreader" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3d5994d1b955407685fe76c7ef7cd0bc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0fa560dfadb74e159c3b7a522baeaa1b"><span data-offset-key="0fa560dfadb74e159c3b7a522baeaa1b:0">Dolphin Screen Reader</span></span></span></a><span key="4b781fe0b0b24db584d39de7cbd73115"><span offset-key="4b781fe0b0b24db584d39de7cbd73115:0"> (Windows).</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="14a80de3e6694bf0b3cb0594771c850c"><span offset-key="14a80de3e6694bf0b3cb0594771c850c:0">Free products, like </span></span><a href="https://www.nvaccess.org" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f3d286166ddc4109a31900910d453fbe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="5bcbd0d4a8a645b59dcc7564c1191a5a"><span data-offset-key="5bcbd0d4a8a645b59dcc7564c1191a5a:0">NVDA</span></span></span></a><span key="e91d3cc1847a47ed9484c1c36a3b0f3a"><span offset-key="e91d3cc1847a47ed9484c1c36a3b0f3a:0"> (Windows), </span></span><a href="https://www.chromevox.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b95ed8288fb74100bab4b62a06d47450" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8787d8adfd03499d9c2d34baf021cfff"><span data-offset-key="8787d8adfd03499d9c2d34baf021cfff:0">ChromeVox</span></span></span></a><span key="103494edcb004032887aa954b65efe62"><span offset-key="103494edcb004032887aa954b65efe62:0"> (Chrome), and </span></span><a href="https://wiki.gnome.org/Projects/Orca" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8eff3ace563c4ce2a04424fe9180e627" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b8be655485f248469fd7125122103891"><span data-offset-key="b8be655485f248469fd7125122103891:0">Orca</span></span></span></a><span key="e59974b92a3a4bf49e9dda84a986b9a6"><span offset-key="e59974b92a3a4bf49e9dda84a986b9a6:0"> (Linux).</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="8b319845f54e444ead85a8ee2e3eb8eb"><span offset-key="8b319845f54e444ead85a8ee2e3eb8eb:0">Software built into the operating system, like </span></span><a href="https://www.apple.com/accessibility/mac/vision/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d113b4f2d69140628311a0caffd6afa9"
