data-offset-key="d04965a867744396a03faa3fbba8101a:0">VoiceOver</span></span></span></a><span key="a8262bc5c3ae4624ae3be2ffac39ddd2"><span offset-key="a8262bc5c3ae4624ae3be2ffac39ddd2:0"> (macOS, iPadOS, iOS), </span></span><a href="https://support.microsoft.com/en-us/help/22798/windows-10-narrator-get-started" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd6a0011ce7a4778bbbacd44a44acc9b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="43f2a3ff3c944febb6823c92676037b1"><span data-offset-key="43f2a3ff3c944febb6823c92676037b1:0">Narrator</span></span></span></a><span key="8c0d3672cc2a408f99bc3b4c7ac87b41"><span offset-key="8c0d3672cc2a408f99bc3b4c7ac87b41:0"> (Windows), </span></span><a href="https://www.chromevox.com" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="24732b0e8d44498ca2d3a007c5f7830e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="6b0b84993a3a4755b17f52a5ad30f40c"><span data-offset-key="6b0b84993a3a4755b17f52a5ad30f40c:0">ChromeVox</span></span></span></a><span key="730ce747807e415b97eeeaf13d3d6e16"><span offset-key="730ce747807e415b97eeeaf13d3d6e16:0"> (on Chrome OS), and </span></span><a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.google.android.marvin.talkback" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c18695ced8db45df8fe6df49c1d553ae" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="2eb79804a14042a197684957a89f2485"><span data-offset-key="2eb79804a14042a197684957a89f2485:0">TalkBack</span></span></span></a><span key="8e539683d85c45e3adb549f519566fae"><span offset-key="8e539683d85c45e3adb549f519566fae:0"> (Android).</span></span>

<span key="d32f143a45854906b732eb6b5ab6746d"><span offset-key="d32f143a45854906b732eb6b5ab6746d:0">It is a good idea to familiarize yourself with screen readers; you should also set up a screen reader and have a play around with it, to get an idea of how it works. See our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#screenreaders" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="962ddc01804f4b508c91f44553ae3d8f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="feed7babcb3846bc99ed3d343799804c"><span data-offset-key="feed7babcb3846bc99ed3d343799804c:0">cross-browser testing screen readers guide</span></span></span></a><span key="4057f36bb96d417aa673e775078de8ef"><span offset-key="4057f36bb96d417aa673e775078de8ef:0"> for more details on using them. The below video also provides a brief example of what the experience is like.</span></span>

<span key="7d3a56a2bbb7423287bd7b944245f847"><span offset-key="7d3a56a2bbb7423287bd7b944245f847:0">In terms of statistics, the World Health Organization estimates that "285 million people are estimated to be visually impaired worldwide: 39 million are blind and 246 million have low vision." (see </span></span><a href="https://www.who.int/mediacentre/factsheets/fs282/en/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8855b428e7bc41fa840d5793c34ff974" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="fec5a544afcf426e97db760831aa60a7"><span data-offset-key="fec5a544afcf426e97db760831aa60a7:0">Visual impairment and blindness</span></span></span></a><span key="2d4f0518e8f743cc8a1679d942c94f4b"><span offset-key="2d4f0518e8f743cc8a1679d942c94f4b:0">). That's a large and significant population of users to just miss out on because your site isn't coded properly â€” almost the same size as the population of the United States of America.</span></span>

### 

<span key="83de1dcebeb443939bfaae46686d7451"><span offset-key="83de1dcebeb443939bfaae46686d7451:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#people_with_hearing_impairments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="51e3e0062b0f4997894bc80d4b2b644f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f5491175c2624969bdec2a9f224b9487"><span data-offset-key="f5491175c2624969bdec2a9f224b9487:0">People with hearing impairments</span></span></span></a><span key="16c2d0fd10a14cc582f08b0a75c61900"><span offset-key="16c2d0fd10a14cc582f08b0a75c61900:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="491942360b174b00b8a62ce538a34110"><span offset-key="491942360b174b00b8a62ce538a34110:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.nad.org/resources/american-sign-language/community-and-culture-frequently-asked-questions/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb984be6f6084cc390b217f3e7960f88" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e5181c9145db47e5a5cd2a750be3b4c8"><span data-offset-key="e5181c9145db47e5a5cd2a750be3b4c8:0">Deaf and hard-of-hearing (DHH)</span></span></span></a><span key="e79a34f760064fe6a1f7b26259027445"><span offset-key="e79a34f760064fe6a1f7b26259027445:0"> people have various levels of hearing loss ranging from mild to profound. Although some do use AT (see </span></span><a href="https://www.nidcd.nih.gov/health/assistive-devices-people-hearing-voice-speech-or-language-disorders" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="83171a8d17ce4547a79a0ae6e34c77a8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="703e5dbd21b94ca889aa706626bfbd94"><span data-offset-key="703e5dbd21b94ca889aa706626bfbd94:0">Assistive Devices for People with Hearing, Voice, Speech, or Language Disorders</span></span></span></a><span key="862a4fb43ead457786d382329f3b0cb1"><span offset-key="862a4fb43ead457786d382329f3b0cb1:0">), they are not widespread..</span></span>

<span key="b671012b28a04bedacbe293af56b2847"><span offset-key="b671012b28a04bedacbe293af56b2847:0">To provide access, textual alternatives must be provided. Videos should be manually captioned, and transcripts should be provided for audio content. Furthermore, due to high levels of </span></span><a href="https://therapytravelers.com/language-deprivation/#:~:text=Language%20deprivation%20is%20the%20term,therefore%20not%20exposed%20to%20language." class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="558f281039b842aaaebdacad8c2c6f2c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="ebf40bcacdaa443d98b007817645768e"><span data-offset-key="ebf40bcacdaa443d98b007817645768e:0">language deprivation</span></span></span></a><span key="4b48ab5815dc49ca967142f077215baf"><span offset-key="4b48ab5815dc49ca967142f077215baf:0"> in DHH populations, </span></span><a href="https://circlcenter.org/collaborative-research-automatic-text-simplification-and-reading-assistance-to-support-self-directed-learning-by-deaf-and-hard-of-hearing-computing-workers/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ea78d9f03ba43e196079ed6f69b2893" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="368b547f34c4485da336f065347e32c0"><span data-offset-key="368b547f34c4485da336f065347e32c0:0">text simplification should be considered</span></span></span></a><span key="e88fd89d7a974cdaa1ff32c29057db1c"><span offset-key="e88fd89d7a974cdaa1ff32c29057db1c:0">.</span></span>

<span key="d03d29c2b24949c8ad2d83115efc9a3f"><span offset-key="d03d29c2b24949c8ad2d83115efc9a3f:0">Deaf and hard-of-hearing people also represent a significant userbase â€” "466 million people worldwide have disabling hearing loss", says the World Health Organization's </span></span><a href="https://www.who.int/mediacentre/factsheets/fs300/en/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc0252bd93694c908281a95b54b6e837" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e043212d14e646a0b07ce04c0c492f9b"><span data-offset-key="e043212d14e646a0b07ce04c0c492f9b:0">Deafness and hearing loss</span></span></span></a><span key="394c413c43c848e6947a4d58d7beb380"><span offset-key="394c413c43c848e6947a4d58d7beb380:0"> fact sheet.</span></span>

### 

<span key="7c1e021bf04f48629a1a222718ec5953"><span offset-key="7c1e021bf04f48629a1a222718ec5953:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#people_with_mobility_impairments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="95cde2a19079400bb8fabc00a077a31d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="05b16b6d90a84e7faa408a2cd4c4885c"><span data-offset-key="05b16b6d90a84e7faa408a2cd4c4885c:0">People with mobility impairments</span></span></span></a><span key="b3836d38442446f39ff43be6023bf544"><span offset-key="b3836d38442446f39ff43be6023bf544:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="54442d7ca8064871b0d9893e84418938"><span offset-key="54442d7ca8064871b0d9893e84418938:0">These people have disabilities concerning movement, which might involve purely physical issues (such as loss of limb or paralysis), or neurological/genetic disorders that lead to weakness or loss of control in limbs. Some people might have difficulty making the exact hand movements required to use a mouse, while others might be more severely affected, perhaps being significantly paralyzed to the point where they need to use a </span></span><a href="https://www.performancehealth.com/baseball-cap-head-pointer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4ac3a79cae9d49ec8765c79120137e89" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b5c24d86693f4ab7865df53bf377696a"><span data-offset-key="b5c24d86693f4ab7865df53bf377696a:0">head pointer</span></span></span></a><span key="048eaa88bf14486f94d3745218b862e2"><span offset-key="048eaa88bf14486f94d3745218b862e2:0"> to interact with computers.</span></span>

<span key="a37c00bcfa044704aa0960608fce9367"><span offset-key="a37c00bcfa044704aa0960608fce9367:0">This kind of disability can also be a result of old age, rather than any specific trauma or condition, and it could also result from hardware limitations â€” some users might not have a mouse.</span></span>

<span key="de8c06ac74a34335ad84c776dc37b344"><span offset-key="de8c06ac74a34335ad84c776dc37b344:0">The way this usually affects web development work is the requirement that controls be accessible by the keyboard â€” we'll discuss keyboard accessibility in later articles in the module, but it is a good idea to try out some websites using just the keyboard to see how you get on. Can you use the Tab key to move between the different controls of a web form, for example? You can find more details about keyboard controls in our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#using_native_keyboard_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f53628bc24d439da8871fd2afcf0eb6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d7089bcae6ca4661b0986a47467396a0"><span data-offset-key="d7089bcae6ca4661b0986a47467396a0:0">Cross browser testing Using native keyboard accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="5e912090d4404466b23698600ff8d457"><span offset-key="5e912090d4404466b23698600ff8d457:0"> section.</span></span>

<span key="d63cf30165334f62b42e1b5ae10d08b1"><span offset-key="d63cf30165334f62b42e1b5ae10d08b1:0">In terms of statistics, a significant number of people have mobility impairments. The US Centers for Disease Control and Prevention </span></span><a href="https://www.cdc.gov/nchs/fastats/disability.htm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5dc6a1525ca04d50ba50682265ad979d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="455302de6ecd42ceb37fa940ad5083be"><span data-offset-key="455302de6ecd42ceb37fa940ad5083be:0">Disability and Functioning (Non-institutionalized Adults 18 Years and Over)</span></span></span></a><span key="90519928ed354e23bc17f480f81a1228"><span offset-key="90519928ed354e23bc17f480f81a1228:0"> reports the USA "Percent of adults with any physical functioning difficulty: 16.1%".</span></span>

### 

<span key="a0be9197207e4c7fa3ab7dc6c28268af"><span offset-key="a0be9197207e4c7fa3ab7dc6c28268af:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#people_with_cognitive_impairments" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="92bdc30379c2414fa3229d2581ef3535" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1b389d8897fc4880aa08629863b7091d"><span data-offset-key="1b389d8897fc4880aa08629863b7091d:0">People with cognitive impairments</span></span></span></a><span key="e2bec6098b494917bb4bc9f88fc93a6b"><span offset-key="e2bec6098b494917bb4bc9f88fc93a6b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="17a775c7dc744c11a17f21e1adffd936"><span offset-key="17a775c7dc744c11a17f21e1adffd936:0">Cognitive impairment refers to a broad range of disabilities, from people with intellectual disabilities who have the most-limited capabilities, to all of us as we age and have difficulty thinking and remembering. The range includes people with mental illnesses, such as </span></span><a href="https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/topics/depression/index.shtml" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="502c27c380964713b070f277df829838" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d9765e846e9d4aff8ca0aa61d5ae3daa"><span data-offset-key="d9765e846e9d4aff8ca0aa61d5ae3daa:0">depression</span></span></span></a><span key="1d51d86709eb4862ac3fe60e64350ae5"><span offset-key="1d51d86709eb4862ac3fe60e64350ae5:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/topics/schizophrenia/index.shtml" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e80f9a02d62c4f84943b39b08c640ef1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3de213ca835a46d58d16cff51e683bb4"><span data-offset-key="3de213ca835a46d58d16cff51e683bb4:0">schizophrenia</span></span></span></a><span key="b510eeeea6cf4fb38504e68209aff182"><span offset-key="b510eeeea6cf4fb38504e68209aff182:0">. It also includes people with learning disabilities, such as </span></span><a href="https://www.ninds.nih.gov/Disorders/All-Disorders/Learning-Disabilities-Information-Page" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c131b2c705da4f199db257d81d4bd1c9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="191f054e05d94956a6fec9ddbf0dc5d6"><span data-offset-key="191f054e05d94956a6fec9ddbf0dc5d6:0">dyslexia</span></span></span></a><span key="6334802613cc4c899d80544be8a18ccf"><span offset-key="6334802613cc4c899d80544be8a18ccf:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.nimh.nih.gov/health/topics/attention-deficit-hyperactivity-disorder-adhd/index.shtml" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e69272452681427aa8a1522b4dc81c35" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f139553d128d4ba087b1b6c3f8b4cf45"><span data-offset-key="f139553d128d4ba087b1b6c3f8b4cf45:0">attention deficit hyperactivity disorder</span></span></span></a><span key="7ba8a8696ed04a5cb22740ea268d6113"><span offset-key="7ba8a8696ed04a5cb22740ea268d6113:0">. Importantly, though there is a lot of diversity within clinical definitions of cognitive impairments, people with them experience a common set of functional problems. These include difficulty with understanding content, remembering how to complete tasks, and confusion caused by inconsistent webpage layouts.</span></span>

<span key="f3502a93f52a4a6d8948e1d9ce056378"><span offset-key="f3502a93f52a4a6d8948e1d9ce056378:0">A good foundation of accessibility for people with cognitive impairments includes:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="eba36652abf34686a2fbf9354582b5df"><span offset-key="eba36652abf34686a2fbf9354582b5df:0">Delivering content in more than one way, such as by text-to-speech or by video.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="665378993f6f4ed99a64b46736a73980"><span offset-key="665378993f6f4ed99a64b46736a73980:0">Easily understood content, such as text written using plain-language standards.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="d00b51add472492aa45518346352dfd6"><span offset-key="d00b51add472492aa45518346352dfd6:0">Focusing attention on important content.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="6c06385d0f3544b88cf1701204c9e514"><span offset-key="6c06385d0f3544b88cf1701204c9e514:0">Minimizing distractions, such as unnecessary content or advertisements.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="31983aa207b344fe852ced536531c2f0"><span offset-key="31983aa207b344fe852ced536531c2f0:0">Consistent webpage layout and navigation.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="51ea7b1e50d748d9acfbac59b9df3c7c"><span offset-key="51ea7b1e50d748d9acfbac59b9df3c7c:0">Familiar elements, such as underlined links blue when not visited and purple when visited.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="5c630425879e48eab2c55e426f04224e"><span offset-key="5c630425879e48eab2c55e426f04224e:0">Dividing processes into logical, essential steps with progress indicators.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="aa998c0db77d44e9bec12952873c6761"><span offset-key="aa998c0db77d44e9bec12952873c6761:0">Website authentication as easy as possible without compromising security.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="8ce878c9df154ba9b67453509c315f21"><span offset-key="8ce878c9df154ba9b67453509c315f21:0">Making forms easy to complete, such as with clear error messages and simple error recovery.</span></span>

### 

<span key="45483646eefe47df9e8c76454f7588d9"><span offset-key="45483646eefe47df9e8c76454f7588d9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#notes" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="737cee176f59423abc2fac48d346f954" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1a8e6a32b0e644718c81f278d3a700ed"><span data-offset-key="1a8e6a32b0e644718c81f278d3a700ed:0">Notes</span></span></span></a><span key="0a6ad08b108b4f55b64bd97069eb73c6"><span offset-key="0a6ad08b108b4f55b64bd97069eb73c6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="c8fc61f9621c46f3a87f96ba83527f1a"><span offset-key="c8fc61f9621c46f3a87f96ba83527f1a:0">Designing with </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Cognitive_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="203afa0a12c840318105e4117daa03b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="196d57314e0343aba82f9caa7ad6b8c0"><span data-offset-key="196d57314e0343aba82f9caa7ad6b8c0:0">cognitive accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="d534f56943c14a369ae24096c0b313f8"><span offset-key="d534f56943c14a369ae24096c0b313f8:0"> will lead to good design practices. They will benefit everyone.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="415e7002dd3b4794a348cfb0e023cc29"><span offset-key="415e7002dd3b4794a348cfb0e023cc29:0">Many people with cognitive impairments also have physical disabilities. Websites must conform with the W3Câ€™s </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/standards-guidelines/wcag/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="479f2641180649b3bfa0096afb9b2d2f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="540ea49dc151480eab4069bfb27ddf87"><span data-offset-key="540ea49dc151480eab4069bfb27ddf87:0">Web Content Accessibility Guidelines</span></span></span></a><span key="e04d81cad2294a4686a56d7ad141e524"><span offset-key="e04d81cad2294a4686a56d7ad141e524:0">, including </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Cognitive_accessibility#guidelines" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ecd71ee917374210be4bf98d7dbe55da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3358661032174a37ac3504e2403826f2"><span data-offset-key="3358661032174a37ac3504e2403826f2:0">cognitive accessibility guidelines</span></span></span></a><span key="50452d1335614e9685caff94740523c4"><span offset-key="50452d1335614e9685caff94740523c4:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="7b85693515ed4cb483fe439dbebf138f"><span offset-key="7b85693515ed4cb483fe439dbebf138f:0">The W3Câ€™s </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/GL/task-forces/coga/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5edbb5fe30ab4b7885641b4f6697816a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="48ab0eb77eab457e80d76da3a50ff11d"><span data-offset-key="48ab0eb77eab457e80d76da3a50ff11d:0">Cognitive and Learning Disabilities Accessibility Task Force</span></span></span></a><span key="92f81c55ed2242928b19a11eb35f92e9"><span offset-key="92f81c55ed2242928b19a11eb35f92e9:0"> produces web accessibility guidelines for people with cognitive impairments.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="f77af9e22c954a7a97af5a2a598740be"><span offset-key="f77af9e22c954a7a97af5a2a598740be:0">WebAIM has a </span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/articles/cognitive/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="877c25e1e20340278cc64914b2560324" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="089c2525eae142e49ed8ff4142c95360"><span data-offset-key="089c2525eae142e49ed8ff4142c95360:0">Cognitive page</span></span></span></a><span key="c6db6ed4b055428aa522d3c5e33335eb"><span offset-key="c6db6ed4b055428aa522d3c5e33335eb:0"> of relevant information and resources.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="64e7e339d9bc40adbf7f57f7230a147f"><span offset-key="64e7e339d9bc40adbf7f57f7230a147f:0">The United States Centers for Disease Control estimate that, as of 2018, 1 in 4 US citizens have a disability and, of them, </span></span><a href="https://www.cdc.gov/media/releases/2018/p0816-disability.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="23073653d5d648e2a588325032d5eae6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="aa3385c2af3742dd9d8df2aa8358eda6"><span data-offset-key="aa3385c2af3742dd9d8df2aa8358eda6:0">cognitive impairment is the most common for young people</span></span></span></a><span key="e8345ef85ad64bdd8ab7f155893904f5"><span offset-key="e8345ef85ad64bdd8ab7f155893904f5:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="736779b7c36c4399ab7cf0a0e4ad88b9"><span offset-key="736779b7c36c4399ab7cf0a0e4ad88b9:0">In the US, some intellectual disabilities have historically been referred to as "mental retardation." Many now consider this term disparaging, so its use should be avoided.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="79e3961d810d43959893d41b79d0bca1"><span offset-key="79e3961d810d43959893d41b79d0bca1:0">In the UK, some intellectual disabilities are referred to as "learning disabilities" or "learning difficulties".</span></span>

## 

<span key="5a251030ccc8408b9538ddb282bd2b6c"><span offset-key="5a251030ccc8408b9538ddb282bd2b6c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#implementing_accessibility_into_your_project" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="be995a7f2ac74ebfb9e8346038274b72" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cf8edf8cb47c440baff663ee40c31f6e"><span data-offset-key="cf8edf8cb47c440baff663ee40c31f6e:0">Implementing accessibility into your project</span></span></span></a><span key="0ab844693fcf4ec291ddefc187f04a36"><span offset-key="0ab844693fcf4ec291ddefc187f04a36:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="130b3103829048cc8936983b35ebbd52"><span offset-key="130b3103829048cc8936983b35ebbd52:0">A common accessibility myth is that accessibility is an expensive "added extra" to implement on a project. This myth actually </span>*can*<span offset-key="130b3103829048cc8936983b35ebbd52:2"> be true if either:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="7182b72b573546ef8d660552a3fdcb88"><span offset-key="7182b72b573546ef8d660552a3fdcb88:0">You are trying to "retrofit" accessibility onto an existing website that has significant accessibility issues.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="69a44cd175634e78bffe664a2d36fb82"><span offset-key="69a44cd175634e78bffe664a2d36fb82:0">You have only started to consider accessibility and uncovered related issues in the late stages of a project.</span></span>

<span key="f3a51c9afd164fbc8fa66a9d3b7d3a7e"><span offset-key="f3a51c9afd164fbc8fa66a9d3b7d3a7e:0">If however, you consider accessibility from the start of a project, the cost of making most content accessible should be fairly minimal.</span></span>

<span key="0a62c258da184ba784840e54471a8c5c"><span offset-key="0a62c258da184ba784840e54471a8c5c:0">When planning your project, factor accessibility testing into your testing regime, just like testing for any other important target audience segment (e.g., target desktop or mobile browsers). Test early and often, ideally running automated tests to pick up on programmatically detectable missing features (such as missing image </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#text_alternatives" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="78bfbcaf4d174da5bb42a8b08a7f85d6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e845e922e5b84f588066df1eee33e70a"><span data-offset-key="e845e922e5b84f588066df1eee33e70a:0">alternative text</span></span></span></a><span key="dabea7170fc84362a1f059ea03ebc172"><span offset-key="dabea7170fc84362a1f059ea03ebc172:0"> or bad link text â€” see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#element_relationships_and_context" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8ad11139fc004f0ea793724851ba78ce" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d1e6fe00c59344dd8a6095a842f1006a"><span data-offset-key="d1e6fe00c59344dd8a6095a842f1006a:0">Element relationships and context</span></span></span></a><span key="d4dc2d46351e49128e64bc1d6b28a515"><span offset-key="d4dc2d46351e49128e64bc1d6b28a515:0">) and doing some testing with disabled user groups to see how well more complex site features work for them. For example:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="b04d9f9b30774197aeb6e92c9b4d1ed2"><span offset-key="b04d9f9b30774197aeb6e92c9b4d1ed2:0">Is my date picker widget usable by people using screen readers?</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="0a6713310b0a4d7bb6c950adf315f1ef"><span offset-key="0a6713310b0a4d7bb6c950adf315f1ef:0">If content updates dynamically, do visually impaired people know about it?</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="5d04ce35c7114b2ea1628a41c33f1b8e"><span offset-key="5d04ce35c7114b2ea1628a41c33f1b8e:0">Are my UI buttons accessible using the keyboard and on touch interfaces?</span></span>

<span key="fdec188f571c4d1b935f8b91f6d6af62"><span offset-key="fdec188f571c4d1b935f8b91f6d6af62:0">You can and should keep a note of potential problem areas in your content that will need work to make it accessible, make sure it is tested thoroughly, and think about solutions/alternatives. Text content (as you'll see in the next article) is easy, but what about your multimedia content, and your whizzy 3D graphics? You should look at your project budget and think about what solutions you have available to make such content accessible. Having all your multimedia content transcribed is one option which, while expensive, is possible.</span></span>

<span key="9ce20fd3e88a413cbe6006bce9d64b0f"><span offset-key="9ce20fd3e88a413cbe6006bce9d64b0f:0">Also, be realistic. "100% accessibility" is an unobtainable ideal â€” you will always come across some kind of edge case that results in a certain user finding certain content difficult to use â€” but you should do as much as you can. If you are planning to include a whizzy 3D pie chart graphic made using WebGL, you might want to include a data table as an accessible alternative representation of the data. Or, you might want to just include the table and get rid of the 3D pie chart â€” the table is accessible by everyone, quicker to code, less CPU-intensive, and easier to maintain.</span></span>

<span key="c4526bfd968e465096a7dcffed2ba585"><span offset-key="c4526bfd968e465096a7dcffed2ba585:0">On the other hand, if you are working on a gallery website showing interesting 3D art, it would be unreasonable to expect every piece of art to be perfectly accessible to visually impaired people, given that it is an entirely visual medium.</span></span>

<span key="f3843a4fb3bb42fb84cd832c9e1e944d"><span offset-key="f3843a4fb3bb42fb84cd832c9e1e944d:0">To show that you care and have thought about accessibility, publish an accessibility statement on your site that details what your policy is toward accessibility, and what steps you have taken toward making the site accessible. If someone does notify you that your site has an accessibility problem, start a dialog with them, be empathetic, and take reasonable steps to try to fix the problem.</span></span>

<span key="b5396324423a4698948cd99653330200">**Note:**<span offset-key="b5396324423a4698948cd99653330200:1"> Our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="47bef803a26c4b3dbbeadaf69c1ab2f7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9f19e140aa8e467488ba48e95950cb30"><span data-offset-key="9f19e140aa8e467488ba48e95950cb30:0">Handling common accessibility problems article</span></span></span></a><span key="16280d53090d4184bfe29363eae23152"><span offset-key="16280d53090d4184bfe29363eae23152:0"> covers accessibility specifics that should be tested in more detail.</span></span>

<span key="ea1f7c40ac36435786d20b64999d7d0c"><span offset-key="ea1f7c40ac36435786d20b64999d7d0c:0">To summarize:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="7c5da95b7aab428f8cf4ef67afd09c6f"><span offset-key="7c5da95b7aab428f8cf4ef67afd09c6f:0">Consider accessibility from the start of a project, and test early and often. Just like any other bug, an accessibility problem becomes more expensive to fix the later it is discovered.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="b08e3bbe4bc34bad9fdc7f918ccbc376"><span offset-key="b08e3bbe4bc34bad9fdc7f918ccbc376:0">Bear in mind that a lot of accessibility best practices benefit everyone, not just users with disabilities. For example, lean semantic markup is not only good for screen readers, but it is also fast to load and performant. This benefits everyone, especially those on mobile devices and/or slow connections.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="d60a068b09744dfbb9bc6bfe3402c985"><span offset-key="d60a068b09744dfbb9bc6bfe3402c985:0">Publish an accessibility statement on your site and engage with people having problems.</span></span>

## 

<span key="735a537123df402bbb89c3413b840e4b"><span offset-key="735a537123df402bbb89c3413b840e4b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#accessibility_guidelines_and_the_law" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="11542579fde84b12af06d4dcfc185dc2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="6016c7e2b9da400da467e812ed099461"><span data-offset-key="6016c7e2b9da400da467e812ed099461:0">Accessibility guidelines and the law</span></span></span></a><span key="660521187f3249ecae8fdbe62dc8f11f"><span offset-key="660521187f3249ecae8fdbe62dc8f11f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="2654f171d8574796a71b565c12b5a74e"><span offset-key="2654f171d8574796a71b565c12b5a74e:0">There are numerous checklists and sets of guidelines available for basing accessibility tests on, which might seem overwhelming at first glance. Our advice is to familiarize yourself with the basic areas in which you need to take care, as well as understanding the high-level structures of the guidelines that are most relevant to you.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="4b3b5b323d96429d8d4652752a18f77e"><span offset-key="4b3b5b323d96429d8d4652752a18f77e:0">For a start, the W3C has published a large and very detailed document that includes very precise, technology-agnostic criteria for accessibility conformance. These are called the </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/standards-guidelines/wcag/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a58c4021a6e145fb99db198e0f613d08" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cf2c49d43bbd4fec91b3f0f972c438bb"><span data-offset-key="cf2c49d43bbd4fec91b3f0f972c438bb:0">Web Content Accessibility Guidelines</span></span></span></a><span key="b622d15f44124c01924af6d79970fdff"><span offset-key="b622d15f44124c01924af6d79970fdff:0"> (WCAG), and they are not a short read by any means. The criteria are split up into four main categories, which specify how implementations can be made perceivable, operable, understandable, and robust. The best place to get a light introduction and start learning is </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/standards-guidelines/wcag/glance/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="338ddbe8564a42ea8e8de7c61013a6f0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b11d99429e0d493bb57725bd9249233f"><span data-offset-key="b11d99429e0d493bb57725bd9249233f:0">WCAG at a Glance</span></span></span></a><span key="a1dbd190f18b4b83b9c6316ae7c38fc7"><span offset-key="a1dbd190f18b4b83b9c6316ae7c38fc7:0">. There is no need to learn all of the WCAG criteria â€” be aware of the major areas of concern, and use a variety of techniques and tools to highlight any areas that don't conform to the WCAG criteria (see below for more).</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="39a959e82c0f46019ea8c3ecc2b7384f"><span offset-key="39a959e82c0f46019ea8c3ecc2b7384f:0">Your country may also have specific legislation governing the need for websites serving their population to be accessible â€” for example </span></span><a href="https://www.etsi.org/deliver/etsi_en/301500_301599/301549/02.01.02_60/en_301549v020102p.pdf" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e7137ea8d0b649708ab2072bb7a9bc31" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a106b9ab76af434697c7df91ca3881fc"><span data-offset-key="a106b9ab76af434697c7df91ca3881fc:0">EN 301 549</span></span></span></a><span key="8b480488daf1420683a75e0d7974820a"><span offset-key="8b480488daf1420683a75e0d7974820a:0"> in the EU, </span></span><a href="https://www.section508.gov/training" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="313770cdd89143989e8e45d5358ec3fc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3f127ca0bc244eeda076ec17c111981b"><span data-offset-key="3f127ca0bc244eeda076ec17c111981b:0">Section 508 of the Rehabilitation Act</span></span></span></a><span key="2308c952f58a4af180fe85954b3a6aef"><span offset-key="2308c952f58a4af180fe85954b3a6aef:0"> in the US, </span></span><a href="https://www.einfach-fuer-alle.de/artikel/bitv_english/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7a71523397f4e2e9eada003eb031e3d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="592b1e5af05748a7beadefa05cc2442d"><span data-offset-key="592b1e5af05748a7beadefa05cc2442d:0">Federal Ordinance on Barrier-Free Information Technology</span></span></span></a><span key="efa90e7138044ccb989f873055f77cc7"><span offset-key="efa90e7138044ccb989f873055f77cc7:0"> in Germany, the </span></span><a href="https://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/2018/952/introduction/made" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f3b5de3eaf0a46b980163296f7cfcf3a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e5947e6ebd7f4d738906d2ee46edcf6f"><span data-offset-key="e5947e6ebd7f4d738906d2ee46edcf6f:0">Accessibility Regulations 2018</span></span></span></a><span key="29d07992bd964739a3bbcf083fb4c594"><span offset-key="29d07992bd964739a3bbcf083fb4c594:0"> in the UK, </span></span><a href="https://www.agid.gov.it/it/design-servizi/accessibilita-siti-web" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="042d0e9a27c342e782da6691e2696092" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cd57c803f1ce40eaa1d65496c78c1de3"><span data-offset-key="cd57c803f1ce40eaa1d65496c78c1de3:0">AccessibilitÃ </span></span></span></a><span key="1a4c17ffa61541fd9bf4d8ddb01f84ec"><span offset-key="1a4c17ffa61541fd9bf4d8ddb01f84ec:0"> in Italy, the </span></span><a href="https://www.humanrights.gov.au/world-wide-web-access-disability-discrimination-act-advisory-notes-ver-41-2014" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8b2877771e9246b89533cae384f4279c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7179e688f7f449e3acca0e4f7ad8226a"><span data-offset-key="7179e688f7f449e3acca0e4f7ad8226a:0">Disability Discrimination Act</span></span></span></a><span key="6fd8ff2936e7424bac4197d8609cb49c"><span offset-key="6fd8ff2936e7424bac4197d8609cb49c:0"> in Australia, etc. The W3C keeps a list of </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/policies/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c1d277588759450a94f8dc741fe74faf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="34b0cc988dc645459d60b05d1e26c6a2"><span data-offset-key="34b0cc988dc645459d60b05d1e26c6a2:0">Web Accessibility Laws &amp; Policies</span></span></span></a><span key="10ff530f6e8c40e3bd157ba0b3863684"><span offset-key="10ff530f6e8c40e3bd157ba0b3863684:0"> by country.</span></span>

<span key="ed1c3304da0240a69c3ae3ee518b0fba"><span offset-key="ed1c3304da0240a69c3ae3ee518b0fba:0">So while the WCAG is a set of guidelines, your country will probably have laws governing web accessibility, or at least the accessibility of services available to the public (which could include websites, television, physical spaces, etc.) It is a good idea to find out what your laws are. If you make no effort to check that your content is accessible, you could be legally liable if people complain.</span></span>

<span key="df3d66cea9614a1e9c0fdad9c732e0c7"><span offset-key="df3d66cea9614a1e9c0fdad9c732e0c7:0">This sounds serious, but really you just need to consider accessibility as the main priority of your web development practices, as outlined above. If in doubt, get advice from a qualified lawyer. We're not going to offer any more advice than this, because we're not lawyers.</span></span>

## 

<span key="595c0d68c2c94fe09bca729b7f3b3527"><span offset-key="595c0d68c2c94fe09bca729b7f3b3527:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#accessibility_apis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="740c7cc0d39f446da4975adb068fe2e9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="152474c1c3844fec8a5865ca2841de31"><span data-offset-key="152474c1c3844fec8a5865ca2841de31:0">Accessibility APIs</span></span></span></a><span key="10d166b5c5854595a5692792b3a87951"><span offset-key="10d166b5c5854595a5692792b3a87951:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="2889cb989d8a4346ad286a0d930f3b6a"><span offset-key="2889cb989d8a4346ad286a0d930f3b6a:0">Web browsers make use of special </span>**accessibility APIs**<span offset-key="2889cb989d8a4346ad286a0d930f3b6a:2"> (provided by the underlying operating system) that expose information useful for assistive technologies (ATs) â€” ATs mostly tend to make use of semantic information, so this information doesn't include things like styling information, or JavaScript. This information is structured in a tree of information called the </span>**accessibility tree**<span offset-key="2889cb989d8a4346ad286a0d930f3b6a:4">.</span></span>

<span key="57b8e0bea03b49e2a129eb97b84f30a6"><span offset-key="57b8e0bea03b49e2a129eb97b84f30a6:0">Different operating systems have different accessibility APIs available :</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="efc07573e656448787ecb0148b0f3e85"><span offset-key="efc07573e656448787ecb0148b0f3e85:0">Windows: MSAA/IAccessible, UIAExpress, IAccessible2</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="4cf93efc3f694b9d9cefa5c37e96e184"><span offset-key="4cf93efc3f694b9d9cefa5c37e96e184:0">Mac OS X: NSAccessibility</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="16ee23212d744f3b9a679bbc3d9b3ce4"><span offset-key="16ee23212d744f3b9a679bbc3d9b3ce4:0">Linux: AT-SPI</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="ab24f33d198a4370b7edda43f6480aca"><span offset-key="ab24f33d198a4370b7edda43f6480aca:0">Android: Accessibility framework</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="518df5d5b2bd4e99bb00eb09f11e20a3"><span offset-key="518df5d5b2bd4e99bb00eb09f11e20a3:0">iOS: UIAccessibility</span></span>

<span key="5aa87cb0bf7e472ea4141c579b6b77cf"><span offset-key="5aa87cb0bf7e472ea4141c579b6b77cf:0">Where the native semantic information provided by the HTML elements in your web apps falls down, you can supplement it with features from the </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5b45e5baaeed40ad938e58b96a8281dd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a604b01eff5248859e92743f4f58e1c2"><span data-offset-key="a604b01eff5248859e92743f4f58e1c2:0">WAI-ARIA specification</span></span></span></a><span key="ba519545fa504d29a78fa89fb3cdf77f"><span offset-key="ba519545fa504d29a78fa89fb3cdf77f:0">, which add semantic information to the accessibility tree to improve accessibility. You can learn a lot more about WAI-ARIA in our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/WAI-ARIA_basics" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2280b8183c5d4f7fb1c8e59bfe30f12b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8c176eadd5eb410282e77aabbc6c1b64"><span data-offset-key="8c176eadd5eb410282e77aabbc6c1b64:0">WAI-ARIA basics</span></span></span></a><span key="63c886f2a98e41a38bf69c8923b08c8e"><span offset-key="63c886f2a98e41a38bf69c8923b08c8e:0"> article.</span></span>

## 

<span key="a915266521b2444082fa88eede93bf36"><span offset-key="a915266521b2444082fa88eede93bf36:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/What_is_accessibility#summary" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e4789fa59e740f1af18b6ecf2275973" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="938d898ec0614fe89b5bce0a44dfd734"><span data-offset-key="938d898ec0614fe89b5bce0a44dfd734:0">Summary</span></span></span></a><span key="24ddc42b2cf34f32bcf621ee08c2987d"><span offset-key="24ddc42b2cf34f32bcf621ee08c2987d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="116c36d0034d4f9ab58a433ff39dad1f"><span offset-key="116c36d0034d4f9ab58a433ff39dad1f:0">This article should have given you a useful high-level overview of accessibility, shown you why it's important, and looked at how you can fit it into your workflow. You should now also have a thirst to learn about the implementation details that can make sites accessible, and we'll start on that in the next section, looking at why HTML is a good basis for accessibility.</span></span>

## 

<span key="b0fa7af9d84748e8b87a812935631323"><span offset-key="b0fa7af9d84748e8b87a812935631323:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#html_and_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9aa0ebc3af964ceb8dc257f799545512" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="732a217cd9614e53859f1db58d0e0f04"><span data-offset-key="732a217cd9614e53859f1db58d0e0f04:0">HTML and accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="67c2d2e5a9db4a019378abdaa62e4413"><span offset-key="67c2d2e5a9db4a019378abdaa62e4413:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="24f580235152448ebe96e8d53236a44c"><span offset-key="24f580235152448ebe96e8d53236a44c:0">As you learn more about HTML â€” read more resources, look at more examples, etc. â€” you'll keep seeing a common theme: the importance of using semantic HTML (sometimes called POSH, or Plain Old Semantic HTML). This means using the correct HTML elements for their intended purpose as much as possible.</span></span>

<span key="5a9655cba2d84994b755c60eb37a1655"><span offset-key="5a9655cba2d84994b755c60eb37a1655:0">You might wonder why this is so important. After all, you can use a combination of CSS and JavaScript to make just about any HTML element behave in whatever way you want. For example, a control button to play a video on your site could be marked up like this:</span></span>

1

<span key="7ec7e31fd93445fba198d1e694a7d135"><span offset-key="7ec7e31fd93445fba198d1e694a7d135:0">&lt;div>Play video&lt;/div></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjciIHN0eWxlPSJ2ZXJ0aWNhbC1hbGlnbjptaWRkbGU7d2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7" />

Copied!

<span key="d144a2e59357412f9a770120ca10bcc5"><span offset-key="d144a2e59357412f9a770120ca10bcc5:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="bd358b3ad04e4e7e911bf3fffbdcb1af"><span offset-key="bd358b3ad04e4e7e911bf3fffbdcb1af:0">But as you'll see in greater detail later on, it makes sense to use the correct element for the job:</span></span>

1

<span key="0bf2a160c27241cb9ef8f2babdd3b04a"><span offset-key="0bf2a160c27241cb9ef8f2babdd3b04a:0">&lt;button>Play video&lt;/button></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="f694f7fcb7384d688e6751d1f1ed97ed"><span offset-key="f694f7fcb7384d688e6751d1f1ed97ed:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="5fb16eb7ab054aa7acecba6b31688624"><span offset-key="5fb16eb7ab054aa7acecba6b31688624:0">Not only do HTML </span>`<button>`<span offset-key="5fb16eb7ab054aa7acecba6b31688624:2">s have some suitable styling applied by default (which you will probably want to override), they also have built-in keyboard accessibility â€” users can navigate between buttons using the Tab key and activate their selection using Return or Enter.</span></span>

<span key="e168f2695441437d9a5ad069df939c02"><span offset-key="e168f2695441437d9a5ad069df939c02:0">Semantic HTML doesn't take any longer to write than non-semantic (bad) markup if you do it consistently from the start of your project. Even better, semantic markup has other benefits beyond accessibility:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="892a9493e1a9433cb0d8c6a5b664535b">**Easier to develop with**<span offset-key="892a9493e1a9433cb0d8c6a5b664535b:1"> â€” as mentioned above, you get some functionality for free, plus it is arguably easier to understand.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="75ab9ff8563a4a709abd491564e033f1">**Better on mobile**<span offset-key="75ab9ff8563a4a709abd491564e033f1:1"> â€” semantic HTML is arguably lighter in file size than non-semantic spaghetti code, and easier to make responsive.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="3aa6507983e14ddfb1b57eaa9242c433">**Good for SEO**<span offset-key="3aa6507983e14ddfb1b57eaa9242c433:1"> â€” search engines give more importance to keywords inside headings, links, etc. than keywords included in non-semantic </span>`<div>`<span offset-key="3aa6507983e14ddfb1b57eaa9242c433:3">s, etc., so your documents will be more findable by customers.</span></span>

<span key="c7e1f3b49f6440edb4ebaca928bd12ac"><span offset-key="c7e1f3b49f6440edb4ebaca928bd12ac:0">Let's get on and look at accessible HTML in more detail.</span></span>

<span key="f776387ec7554faaa6fa4b084ceb40c6">**Note:**<span offset-key="f776387ec7554faaa6fa4b084ceb40c6:1"> It is a good idea to have a screen reader set up on your local computer so that you can do some testing of the examples shown below. See our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#screenreaders" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="666b95bbb6e94e6199f901be21ad7224" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="20730360eced4f199254d0acb3b87b73"><span data-offset-key="20730360eced4f199254d0acb3b87b73:0">Screen readers guide</span></span></span></a><span key="e8949cb4b3874e0bb0bb848a02550e0d"><span offset-key="e8949cb4b3874e0bb0bb848a02550e0d:0"> for more details.</span></span>

## 

<span key="46c27c4938eb484a955846d40161fbf9"><span offset-key="46c27c4938eb484a955846d40161fbf9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#good_semantics" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f7f0f05228894181ac34cb88583e59a7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="974a4834bb994485924cea2341298b4a"><span data-offset-key="974a4834bb994485924cea2341298b4a:0">Good semantics</span></span></span></a><span key="531a8337e2854c8797ac15983ca7638d"><span offset-key="531a8337e2854c8797ac15983ca7638d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f46f33fc59224ae984f5cc4027caa3b1"><span offset-key="f46f33fc59224ae984f5cc4027caa3b1:0">We've already talked about the importance of proper semantics, and why we should use the right HTML element for the job. This cannot be ignored, as it is one of the main places that accessibility is badly broken if not handled properly.</span></span>

<span key="9596ce33efa645b5906e260e6c0fba05"><span offset-key="9596ce33efa645b5906e260e6c0fba05:0">Out there on the web, the truth is that people do some very strange things with HTML markup. Some abuses of HTML are due to legacy practices that have not been completely forgotten, and some are just plain ignorance. Whatever the case, you should replace such bad code.</span></span>

<span key="84b6f21277ca4a8ab8481e8d61ab0f41"><span offset-key="84b6f21277ca4a8ab8481e8d61ab0f41:0">Sometimes you are not in the position to get rid of lousy markup â€” your pages might be generated by some kind of server-side framework over which you don't have full control, or you might have third party content on your page (such as ad banners) over which you have no control.</span></span>

<span key="76d41105842d4015a865b578c2f57bc0"><span offset-key="76d41105842d4015a865b578c2f57bc0:0">The goal isn't "all or nothing"; every improvement you can make will help the cause of accessibility.</span></span>

### 

<span key="6dd1037a11db4345b443b691b0c6b8a3"><span offset-key="6dd1037a11db4345b443b691b0c6b8a3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#text_content" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cda73db6c94e4b5a9d240700c4c6fc33" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="fbee4b3ee3a942b8bc688a706b109287"><span data-offset-key="fbee4b3ee3a942b8bc688a706b109287:0">Text content</span></span></span></a><span key="53ae160bdc6d4180873f1e08edf97584"><span offset-key="53ae160bdc6d4180873f1e08edf97584:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="46531369fd1747e69854a83e30bba3c8"><span offset-key="46531369fd1747e69854a83e30bba3c8:0">One of the best accessibility aids a screen reader user can have is an excellent content structure with headings, paragraphs, lists, etc. An excellent semantic example might look something like the following:</span></span>

1

<span key="64948fec7cbe41b4a5606630d157c302"><span offset-key="64948fec7cbe41b4a5606630d157c302:0">&lt;h1>My heading&lt;/h1></span></span>

2

<span key="9b8c72bbdba548c286cc4fcb212eead0"><span offset-key="9b8c72bbdba548c286cc4fcb212eead0:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span key="6c40cfaee9aa489ab35c6839c28c2f70"><span offset-key="6c40cfaee9aa489ab35c6839c28c2f70:0">&lt;p>This is the first section of my document.&lt;/p></span></span>

4

<span key="5f7b311a16f14249bf8231115815867f"><span offset-key="5f7b311a16f14249bf8231115815867f:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

5

<span key="1165c05b7b9547d5b9b2d914e7b99e13"><span offset-key="1165c05b7b9547d5b9b2d914e7b99e13:0">&lt;p>I'll add another paragraph here too.&lt;/p></span></span>

6

<span key="e529b7f7337e42bfb7d8e87482704484"><span offset-key="e529b7f7337e42bfb7d8e87482704484:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

7

<span key="f46bf1b769cb453ab50e7df5d0da07e6"><span offset-key="f46bf1b769cb453ab50e7df5d0da07e6:0">&lt;ol></span></span>

8

<span key="aa1efa1722ba4c848e200a00f285a7f2"><span offset-key="aa1efa1722ba4c848e200a00f285a7f2:0"> &lt;li>Here is&lt;/li></span></span>

9

<span key="c37d584bdb1448c79722783e0d13bb1f"><span offset-key="c37d584bdb1448c79722783e0d13bb1f:0"> &lt;li>a list for&lt;/li></span></span>

10

<span key="621fb7ce2c8241848ef255a34fb71a7a"><span offset-key="621fb7ce2c8241848ef255a34fb71a7a:0"> &lt;li>you to read&lt;/li></span></span>

11

<span key="cf3056df3dea4cf8b9b5b50af71ccc9c"><span offset-key="cf3056df3dea4cf8b9b5b50af71ccc9c:0">&lt;/ol></span></span>

12

<span key="8f2e6b0cad344683ac7dda06104bc3c7"><span offset-key="8f2e6b0cad344683ac7dda06104bc3c7:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

13

<span key="8bcd105d2c5e47c0bacb9aa0957dd21f"><span offset-key="8bcd105d2c5e47c0bacb9aa0957dd21f:0">&lt;h2>My subheading&lt;/h2></span></span>

14

<span key="dcfc840ab45c46eaadb4d3c24d28f62c"><span offset-key="dcfc840ab45c46eaadb4d3c24d28f62c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="9c9ed3e50614418bbccb1ad32de3f543"><span offset-key="9c9ed3e50614418bbccb1ad32de3f543:0">&lt;p>This is the first subsection of my document. I'd love people to be able to find this content!&lt;/p></span></span>

16

<span key="5c08c2786fb3411eab38466462ba2af8"><span offset-key="5c08c2786fb3411eab38466462ba2af8:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

17

<span key="5504dac6073c4f708c6bcded9e42f07d"><span offset-key="5504dac6073c4f708c6bcded9e42f07d:0">&lt;h2>My 2nd subheading&lt;/h2></span></span>

18

<span key="334379dce3544fedb895c5638a37a429"><span offset-key="334379dce3544fedb895c5638a37a429:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

19

<span key="a2406584f8d649428c251ad9096c9374"><span offset-key="a2406584f8d649428c251ad9096c9374:0">&lt;p>This is the second subsection of my content. I think is more interesting than the last one.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="cfb7d82162a44e7ea1410d8f7d0dddfa"><span offset-key="cfb7d82162a44e7ea1410d8f7d0dddfa:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="cd8cd446ebbb4feab9ce296dd489abd8"><span offset-key="cd8cd446ebbb4feab9ce296dd489abd8:0">We've prepared a version with longer text for you to try out with a screen reader (see </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/good-semantics.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bed0b31886c945bcab36310e4856a1b5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="ba20c0ae66544bbfa4cdb0b499510ff4"><span data-offset-key="ba20c0ae66544bbfa4cdb0b499510ff4:0">good-semantics.html</span></span></span></a><span key="e1c8a8de464948ca99da1d785df91e86"><span offset-key="e1c8a8de464948ca99da1d785df91e86:0">). If you try navigating through this, you'll see that this is pretty easy to navigate:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="de90630278aa4939916cff9780383ce1"><span offset-key="de90630278aa4939916cff9780383ce1:0">The screen reader reads each header out as you progress through the content, notifying you what a heading is, what is a paragraph, etc.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="0885e12818ba426dac2f663cba001d6b"><span offset-key="0885e12818ba426dac2f663cba001d6b:0">It stops after each element, letting you go at whatever pace is comfortable for you.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="f52bc44c6f3d4569be4e9a983650fea4"><span offset-key="f52bc44c6f3d4569be4e9a983650fea4:0">You can jump to the next/previous heading in many screen readers.</span></span>

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="64d683e047f3471fbe08f600f130c5a2"><span offset-key="64d683e047f3471fbe08f600f130c5a2:0">You can also bring up a list of all headings in many screen readers, allowing you to use them as a handy table of contents to find specific content.</span></span>

<span key="05680ff5d0154fe8ab687960e944bb5c"><span offset-key="05680ff5d0154fe8ab687960e944bb5c:0">People sometimes write headings, paragraphs, etc. using presentational HTML and line breaks, something like the following:</span></span>

1

<span key="228c29d38ed3460d96e72e939dbc4c41"><span offset-key="228c29d38ed3460d96e72e939dbc4c41:0">&lt;font size="7">My heading&lt;/font></span></span>

2

<span key="5f03e1864d6c42fd98325a9297f21e94"><span offset-key="5f03e1864d6c42fd98325a9297f21e94:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

3

<span key="31ec09a5d34f491295380750d65d4f9b"><span offset-key="31ec09a5d34f491295380750d65d4f9b:0">This is the first section of my document.</span></span>

4

<span key="5c3a9590b1df488790bf79affba2c545"><span offset-key="5c3a9590b1df488790bf79affba2c545:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

5

<span key="5694be65496a49079d34714f808be190"><span offset-key="5694be65496a49079d34714f808be190:0">I'll add another paragraph here too.</span></span>

6

<span key="c82587a29a4a451d8546b3a382adb293"><span offset-key="c82587a29a4a451d8546b3a382adb293:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

7

<span key="97876765afe04087bcdbe25c8d9b9a05"><span offset-key="97876765afe04087bcdbe25c8d9b9a05:0">1. Here is</span></span>

8

9

<span key="5dec49d2f88b415382297b207c640fe8"><span offset-key="5dec49d2f88b415382297b207c640fe8:0">2. a list for</span></span>

10

<span key="0fe8cf46dea9496a94f9020e029b5a52"><span offset-key="0fe8cf46dea9496a94f9020e029b5a52:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

<span key="0a893d8429d44f538e206234ef174db3"><span offset-key="0a893d8429d44f538e206234ef174db3:0">3. you to read</span></span>

<span key="61448585c90340da83f7f1f6619f5457"><span offset-key="61448585c90340da83f7f1f6619f5457:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

<span key="7411dff0310e40e589a2312cbd337d75"><span offset-key="7411dff0310e40e589a2312cbd337d75:0">&lt;font size="5">My subheading&lt;/font></span></span>

15

<span key="f78660e0d83240b7a2383bcf50083052"><span offset-key="f78660e0d83240b7a2383bcf50083052:0">This is the first subsection of my document. I'd love people to be able to find this content!</span></span>

<span key="b9f0a5195c6c4c138102562592757475"><span offset-key="b9f0a5195c6c4c138102562592757475:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

<span key="8b5442f571ab48bcb67c90eb801bc7d8"><span offset-key="8b5442f571ab48bcb67c90eb801bc7d8:0">&lt;font size="5">My 2nd subheading&lt;/font></span></span>
