<span key="165a85e3d90446a7bd9d94b878503108"><span offset-key="165a85e3d90446a7bd9d94b878503108:0">&lt;br>&lt;br></span></span>

19

<span key="4e129751518a45fb86daa312ac793082"><span offset-key="4e129751518a45fb86daa312ac793082:0">This is the second subsection of my content. I think is more interesting than the last one.</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="96fe1f7cc3514166972c541335fa3465"><span offset-key="96fe1f7cc3514166972c541335fa3465:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="ced7067182244ef7a05e2231675dfe19"><span offset-key="ced7067182244ef7a05e2231675dfe19:0">If you try our longer version out with a screen reader (see </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/bad-semantics.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b8c25d563959468a888b2ce2cf480193" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="817c261475274c9dacf4e942bcb317fe"><span data-offset-key="817c261475274c9dacf4e942bcb317fe:0">bad-semantics.html</span></span></span></a><span key="f9aa725ff9d94684a1bb965a8f0250cd"><span offset-key="f9aa725ff9d94684a1bb965a8f0250cd:0">), you'll not have a very good experience â€” the screen reader hasn't got anything to use as signposts, so you can't retrieve a useful table of contents, and the whole page is seen as a single giant block, so it is just read out in one go, all at once.</span></span>

<span key="566a116f4771471c9682d6da9e4bada2"><span offset-key="566a116f4771471c9682d6da9e4bada2:0">There are other issues too beyond accessibility â€” it is harder to style the content using CSS, or manipulate it with JavaScript, for example, because there are no elements to use as selectors.</span></span>

<span key="47c9a325491947ea8cb474ba85f31ca0">**Using clear language**</span>

<span key="fa97f3b4b4c24797b719985523b9a6e0"><span offset-key="fa97f3b4b4c24797b719985523b9a6e0:0">The language you use can also affect accessibility. In general, you should use clear language that is not overly complex and doesn't use unnecessary jargon or slang terms. This not only benefits people with cognitive or other disabilities; it benefits readers for whom the text is not written in their first language, younger people ... everyone, in fact! Apart from this, you should try to avoid using language and characters that don't get read out clearly by the screen reader. For example:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="af470ce615c3422fac32383597974190"><span offset-key="af470ce615c3422fac32383597974190:0">Don't use dashes if you can avoid it. Instead of writing 5â€“7, write 5 to 7.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="f7b33a9333ff49b6a330efaac6366e56"><span offset-key="f7b33a9333ff49b6a330efaac6366e56:0">Expand abbreviations â€” instead of writing Jan, write January.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a53a6589960b4b64961aea53b6a67a77"><span offset-key="a53a6589960b4b64961aea53b6a67a77:0">Expand acronyms, at least once or twice. Instead of writing HTML in the first instance, write Hypertext Markup Language.</span></span>

### 

<span key="6c4f0e4de74d44bb901091b2bb5d47a4"><span offset-key="6c4f0e4de74d44bb901091b2bb5d47a4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#page_layouts" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6737313ac829479c8226b03a6aaa1e33" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="2a4f388a07394235a490f99076db7af4"><span data-offset-key="2a4f388a07394235a490f99076db7af4:0">Page layouts</span></span></span></a><span key="92897c727d2d40c6914f15fd73e56e61"><span offset-key="92897c727d2d40c6914f15fd73e56e61:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="508cdee2ace44c488750387edb57be60"><span offset-key="508cdee2ace44c488750387edb57be60:0">In the bad old days, people used to create page layouts using HTML tables â€” using different table cells to contain the header, footer, sidebar, main content column, etc. This is not a good idea because a screen reader will likely give out confusing readouts, especially if the layout is complex and has many nested tables.</span></span>

<span key="abe833777379486796790d95cb9086d5"><span offset-key="abe833777379486796790d95cb9086d5:0">Try our example </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/table-layout.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8500fca1eb164fbbadfa9ce270e83b6b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7898d4504cf0427894db17f596ab6fdc"><span data-offset-key="7898d4504cf0427894db17f596ab6fdc:0">table-layout.html</span></span></span></a><span key="f3dbbc0492f14ddf85df62d9d215273d"><span offset-key="f3dbbc0492f14ddf85df62d9d215273d:0"> example, which looks something like this:</span></span>

1

<span key="9d32a94f3eea42dc89eb521a876f01f2"><span offset-key="9d32a94f3eea42dc89eb521a876f01f2:0">&lt;table width="1200"></span></span>

2

<span key="72bbcd2cfe544271a7972554de017525"><span offset-key="72bbcd2cfe544271a7972554de017525:0">If you try to navigate this using a screen reader, it will probably tell you that there's a table to be looked at (although some screen readers can guess the difference between table layouts and data tables). You'll then likely (depending on which screen reader you're using) have to go down into the table as an object and look at its features separately, then get out of the table again to carry on navigating the content.</span></span>

<span key="4230a3706f4c427da9a18b4810bcdb41"><span offset-key="4230a3706f4c427da9a18b4810bcdb41:0">Table layouts are a relic of the past â€” they made sense back when CSS support was not widespread in browsers, but now they just create confusion for screen reader users. Additionally, their source code requires more markup, which makes them less flexible and more difficult to maintain. You can verify these claims by comparing your previous experience with a </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/html/introduction-to-html/document_and_website_structure/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3fe66940ca114cb3a867fca780c2e523" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0257a12efd894d9cb81011eb3f9ef670"><span data-offset-key="0257a12efd894d9cb81011eb3f9ef670:0">more modern website structure example</span></span></span></a><span key="0085f41f9eef49c39fffa7efd996a3ff"><span offset-key="0085f41f9eef49c39fffa7efd996a3ff:0">, which could look something like this:</span></span>

<span key="df6d4f753a6f47bb8900e76ade8a353f"><span offset-key="df6d4f753a6f47bb8900e76ade8a353f:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="893b1cdb0e7e4abfbdffebefce91e718"><span offset-key="893b1cdb0e7e4abfbdffebefce91e718:0">If you try our more modern structure example with a screen reader, you'll see that the layout markup no longer gets in the way and confuses the content readout. It is also much leaner and smaller in terms of code size, which means easier to maintain code, and less bandwidth for the user to download (particularly prevalent for those on slow connections).</span></span>

<span key="6a2f22083a604dd5b64886e95d6828d3"><span offset-key="6a2f22083a604dd5b64886e95d6828d3:0">Another consideration when creating layouts is using HTML5 semantic elements as seen in the above example (see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element#content_sectioning" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1fd71c2a766a47979c66050635a8adc2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1e2745e80ca8431ca0aa4daad61d99a4"><span data-offset-key="1e2745e80ca8431ca0aa4daad61d99a4:0">content sectioning</span></span></span></a><span key="86f45c4740ec44dcbb483e9d4d61accd"><span offset-key="86f45c4740ec44dcbb483e9d4d61accd:0">) â€” you can create a layout using only nested </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/div" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7de9c371422c4639974b3dfa8d681fef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="5d88fd6ac7f441c883668599bf2f5a61"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="5d88fd6ac7f441c883668599bf2f5a61:0">&lt;div&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="5a830e317713448d9e41cf88648dade2"><span offset-key="5a830e317713448d9e41cf88648dade2:0"> elements, but it is better to use appropriate sectioning elements to wrap your main navigation (</span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/nav" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fd978339f6574837b4972ddb5b730bdc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="5f5f7fc09b4e420b90e24a518f3fb245"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="5f5f7fc09b4e420b90e24a518f3fb245:0">&lt;nav&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="6c038b71e58542c693c788ed4ef5c17b"><span offset-key="6c038b71e58542c693c788ed4ef5c17b:0">), footer (</span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/footer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a116f166cb134e55afbb514316fa6935" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="76696a15ebc9431daf80b00ff36024d5"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="76696a15ebc9431daf80b00ff36024d5:0">&lt;footer&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="bd66de711b41487795f894dbd8eadeff"><span offset-key="bd66de711b41487795f894dbd8eadeff:0">), repeating content units (</span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/article" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c6b3c953cc8d4627b8d2f6ba4acdc5f2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f9f6f8681d0a4ad295484cb279d7e36f"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="f9f6f8681d0a4ad295484cb279d7e36f:0">&lt;article&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="316e02ca611d42a8b9082ae602721018"><span offset-key="316e02ca611d42a8b9082ae602721018:0">), etc. These provide extra semantics for screen readers (and other tools) to give user extra clues about the content they are navigating (see </span></span><a href="https://www.weba11y.com/blog/2016/04/22/screen-reader-support-for-new-html5-section-elements/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c382b346e8844bfb83d3f36ec8c2bd7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8478ca19d10d4cbdbb23cf5ce0210ddd"><span data-offset-key="8478ca19d10d4cbdbb23cf5ce0210ddd:0">Screen Reader Support for new HTML5 Section Elements</span></span></span></a><span key="2b98cdcc2a2f4e56916944f08a9f9e97"><span offset-key="2b98cdcc2a2f4e56916944f08a9f9e97:0"> for an idea of what screen reader support is like).</span></span>

<span key="b87d684cd3f741c6a1e50a46e0b2bdce">**Note:**<span offset-key="b87d684cd3f741c6a1e50a46e0b2bdce:1"> In addition to having good semantics and an attractive layout, your content should make logical sense in its source order â€” you can always place it where you want using CSS later on, but you should get the source order right to start with, so what screen reader users get read out to them will make sense.</span></span>

### 

<span key="8649c328b53f4354bd3dd61bb7bd20c5"><span offset-key="8649c328b53f4354bd3dd61bb7bd20c5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#ui_controls" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d2da886496f04b1fbd735728616988b7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="fb84387622654018bf1273e2f8eb0a49"><span data-offset-key="fb84387622654018bf1273e2f8eb0a49:0">UI controls</span></span></span></a><span key="68259b6a68e84a739e2a50d155e4c448"><span offset-key="68259b6a68e84a739e2a50d155e4c448:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="a9c8573ab8a1499e8fe4ad67c69143e2"><span offset-key="a9c8573ab8a1499e8fe4ad67c69143e2:0">By UI controls, we mean the main parts of web documents that users interact with â€” most commonly buttons, links, and form controls. In this section, we'll look at the basic accessibility concerns to be aware of when creating such controls. Later articles on WAI-ARIA and multimedia will look at other aspects of UI accessibility.</span></span>

<span key="f27f546737764e208678be6c11f760ff"><span offset-key="f27f546737764e208678be6c11f760ff:0">One key aspect of the accessibility of UI controls is that by default, browsers allow them to be manipulated by the keyboard. You can try this out using our </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/tools-testing/cross-browser-testing/accessibility/native-keyboard-accessibility.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f50cf43721344e37a35becaf749b9234" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="31f9a54835f04a0f8b072f7c6bea68cc"><span data-offset-key="31f9a54835f04a0f8b072f7c6bea68cc:0">native-keyboard-accessibility.html</span></span></span></a><span key="88ee14edc3c44058aa8ebfcf815750e4"><span offset-key="88ee14edc3c44058aa8ebfcf815750e4:0"> example (see the </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/tools-testing/cross-browser-testing/accessibility/native-keyboard-accessibility.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="138220e5629c4d8196dbbffbb898ad18" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8a51306aff62455d8b0337862018923c"><span data-offset-key="8a51306aff62455d8b0337862018923c:0">source code</span></span></span></a><span key="4493a67a0dc347f99fdf744cf6908618"><span offset-key="4493a67a0dc347f99fdf744cf6908618:0">). Open this in a new tab, and try pressing the tab key; after a few presses, you should see the tab focus start to move through the different focusable elements. The focused elements are given a highlighted default style in every browser (it differs slightly between different browsers) so that you can tell what element is focused.</span></span>

<span key="014c23414fb94260b290c4d76f2b56e0"><span offset-key="014c23414fb94260b290c4d76f2b56e0:0">From Firefox 84 you can also enable an overlay that shows the page tabbing order. For more information see: </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Tools/Accessibility_inspector#show_web_page_tabbing_order" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="637c17cd0fcc4f60ada04476a11b6485" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="2ff9e9c4d6cf48d186676a757e80ae50"><span data-offset-key="2ff9e9c4d6cf48d186676a757e80ae50:0">Accessibility Inspector &gt; Show web page tabbing order</span></span></span></a><span key="b8ba7efcee80400db073f4c0deeef2ff"><span offset-key="b8ba7efcee80400db073f4c0deeef2ff:0">.</span></span>

<span key="27771688791e4d83b175749ad4cc218a"><span offset-key="27771688791e4d83b175749ad4cc218a:0">You can then press Enter/Return to follow a focused link or press a button (we've included some JavaScript to make the buttons alert a message), or start typing to enter text in a text input. Other form elements have different controls, for example, the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/select" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4712c53588e34dd6a92a753282b99e2d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e6f9195e60c344f98e6fb0c4c1fa044f"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="e6f9195e60c344f98e6fb0c4c1fa044f:0">&lt;select&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="f7b9457dee0f4bb7b5acb02b2ba221b9"><span offset-key="f7b9457dee0f4bb7b5acb02b2ba221b9:0"> element can have its options displayed and cycled between using the up and down arrow keys.</span></span>

<span key="3183d9645e954575bf826cadabbb6390">**Note:**<span offset-key="3183d9645e954575bf826cadabbb6390:1"> Different browsers may have different keyboard control options available. See </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Tools_and_testing/Cross_browser_testing/Accessibility#using_native_keyboard_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="01343fd0122241d6a2e8b04a72649086" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d83b572f465b487db885c91f34fe2c10"><span data-offset-key="d83b572f465b487db885c91f34fe2c10:0">Using native keyboard accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="86dcf019b7ec444185dda763212c3be7"><span offset-key="86dcf019b7ec444185dda763212c3be7:0"> for more details.</span></span>

<span key="332267d44e2b44e1a57c2f2e601a929b"><span offset-key="332267d44e2b44e1a57c2f2e601a929b:0">You essentially get this behavior for free, just by using the appropriate elements, e.g.</span></span>

<span key="ffe1b53d21cf4883892a63090dcf746c"><span offset-key="ffe1b53d21cf4883892a63090dcf746c:0">This means using links, buttons, form elements, and labels appropriately (including the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/label" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ff298ed03ce144ed851189c9a78d2b7f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="17728750fea249e799749220db44eb4c"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="17728750fea249e799749220db44eb4c:0">&lt;label&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="e584b404581f4d979df0b200f1766c80"><span offset-key="e584b404581f4d979df0b200f1766c80:0"> element for form controls).</span></span>

<span key="126eedeac9f946a3828ff2de32652623"><span offset-key="126eedeac9f946a3828ff2de32652623:0">However, it is again the case that people sometimes do strange things with HTML. For example, you sometimes see buttons marked up using </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/div" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="32c19a2aeb094af7a89469fef2489983" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="49ded44acee94fb998f34c26116025a6"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="49ded44acee94fb998f34c26116025a6:0">&lt;div&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="37e1bfae274645c4b82199a5a7d61eb7"><span offset-key="37e1bfae274645c4b82199a5a7d61eb7:0">s, for example:</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="1bf719b175144583a4968addfb6b492d"><span offset-key="1bf719b175144583a4968addfb6b492d:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="9e87bfbf45d04c758ace0bd165b59451"><span offset-key="9e87bfbf45d04c758ace0bd165b59451:0">But using such code is not advised â€” you immediately lose the native keyboard accessibility you would have had if you'd just used </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/button" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c292fad37c1d4ff286191bc085b7cac3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="92818a0ab746468da207dc24d2489ecd"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="92818a0ab746468da207dc24d2489ecd:0">&lt;button&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="f03269d5d81048049a122870b3d8ef79"><span offset-key="f03269d5d81048049a122870b3d8ef79:0"> elements, plus you don't get any of the default CSS styling that buttons get.</span></span>

<span key="b5ab486124ea46caa8c3440a34f760f9">**Building keyboard accessibility back in**</span>

<span key="6df0d7b5bc0742c7be54fafd9a002226"><span offset-key="6df0d7b5bc0742c7be54fafd9a002226:0">Adding such advantages back in takes a bit of work (you can see an example in our </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/tools-testing/cross-browser-testing/accessibility/fake-div-buttons.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bf09c2c89ebe4c1f9b4a4e833b136e85" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9991ee2720894a1ab5e305624cca6305"><span data-offset-key="9991ee2720894a1ab5e305624cca6305:0">fake-div-buttons.html</span></span></span></a><span key="33f4864e0f044ef286cc85745b347ecd"><span offset-key="33f4864e0f044ef286cc85745b347ecd:0"> example â€” also see the </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/tools-testing/cross-browser-testing/accessibility/fake-div-buttons.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="196c07274b3247ceb5d1fd2313083b6c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e009b492d9764706b599b124deb4ab4e"><span data-offset-key="e009b492d9764706b599b124deb4ab4e:0">source code</span></span></span></a><span key="bd5784415dfd46c59dc3b499d0444387"><span offset-key="bd5784415dfd46c59dc3b499d0444387:0">). Here we've given our fake </span>`<div>`<span offset-key="bd5784415dfd46c59dc3b499d0444387:2"> buttons the ability to be focused (including via tab) by giving each one the attribute </span>`tabindex="0"`<span offset-key="bd5784415dfd46c59dc3b499d0444387:4">:</span></span>

1

<span key="0f57d6dbe8224715a542ae4ec7764934"><span offset-key="0f57d6dbe8224715a542ae4ec7764934:0">&lt;div data-message="This is from the first button" tabindex="0">Click me!&lt;/div></span></span>

2

<span key="14d2afda88814977abd65f7afe84e8d4"><span offset-key="14d2afda88814977abd65f7afe84e8d4:0">&lt;div data-message="This is from the second button" tabindex="0">Click me too!&lt;/div></span></span>

3

<span key="3e1c5cfa414449208de83ca1c3cccfb0"><span offset-key="3e1c5cfa414449208de83ca1c3cccfb0:0">&lt;div data-message="This is from the third button" tabindex="0">And me!&lt;/div></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="0b47c731e88a49588e5bc46f63706054"><span offset-key="0b47c731e88a49588e5bc46f63706054:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="41fc448c3bc842a7804f11af8a1ff4b0"><span offset-key="41fc448c3bc842a7804f11af8a1ff4b0:0">Basically, the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Global_attributes#attr-tabindex" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7006a17d79814625bbd5805cd46a726f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="6c6d28c74a12453291c334ecccf66446"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="6c6d28c74a12453291c334ecccf66446:0">tabindex</code></span></span></a><span key="705f6f037ca24f6187d65d9f2431274f"><span offset-key="705f6f037ca24f6187d65d9f2431274f:0"> attribute is primarily intended to allow tabbable elements to have a custom tab order (specified in positive numerical order), instead of just being tabbed through in their default source order. This is nearly always a bad idea, as it can cause major confusion. Use it only if you really need to, for example, if the layout shows things in a very different visual order to the source code, and you want to make things work more logically. There are two other options for </span>`tabindex`<span offset-key="705f6f037ca24f6187d65d9f2431274f:2">:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7f350859f5e04bbfb84babddc2de1d2f">`tabindex="0"`<span offset-key="7f350859f5e04bbfb84babddc2de1d2f:1"> â€” as indicated above, this value allows elements that are not normally tabbable to become tabbable. This is the most useful value of </span>`tabindex`<span offset-key="7f350859f5e04bbfb84babddc2de1d2f:3">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="60beb79aada9420b951e691d760a449b">`tabindex="-1"`<span offset-key="60beb79aada9420b951e691d760a449b:1"> â€” this allows not normally tabbable elements to receive focus programmatically, e.g., via JavaScript, or as the target of links.</span></span>

<span key="bfe2f9905ef74ec09d514ace5356983d"><span offset-key="bfe2f9905ef74ec09d514ace5356983d:0">Whilst the above addition allows us to tab to the buttons, it does not allow us to activate them via the Enter/Return key. To do that, we had to add the following bit of JavaScript trickery:</span></span>

1

<span key="6666d4d6b5e644feb9f22daaafe07804"><span offset-key="6666d4d6b5e644feb9f22daaafe07804:0">document.onkeydown = function(e) {</span></span>

2

<span key="d343ed674fd149f7bcdcb3c194d7adb6"><span offset-key="d343ed674fd149f7bcdcb3c194d7adb6:0"> if(e.keyCode === 13) { // The Enter/Return key</span></span>

3

<span key="25248b39518748e1bb5820ba2a09c2bb"><span offset-key="25248b39518748e1bb5820ba2a09c2bb:0"> document.activeElement.click();</span></span>

4

<span key="5636d22cbf4741c8886eed5be1495f25"><span offset-key="5636d22cbf4741c8886eed5be1495f25:0"> }</span></span>

5

<span key="c3920939dd92415780a8cab48d31dfbd"><span offset-key="c3920939dd92415780a8cab48d31dfbd:0">};</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="b69dd6c2391b4377bb616b861d0cec70"><span offset-key="b69dd6c2391b4377bb616b861d0cec70:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="a78b07c4de4044f3a82c00c1a53294ec"><span offset-key="a78b07c4de4044f3a82c00c1a53294ec:0">Here we add a listener to the </span>`document`<span offset-key="a78b07c4de4044f3a82c00c1a53294ec:2"> object to detect when a button has been pressed on the keyboard. We check what button was pressed via the event object's </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/KeyboardEvent/keyCode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5cc4126c339e49479081a0068d9f2a4c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9fad4e56b4de4b4a8bd3c7dbdc13d7d6"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="9fad4e56b4de4b4a8bd3c7dbdc13d7d6:0">keyCode</code></span></span></a><span key="9990e0003f304a5fa72ec9e1bab61e32"><span offset-key="9990e0003f304a5fa72ec9e1bab61e32:0"> property; if it is the keycode that matches Return/Enter, we run the function stored in the button's </span>`onclick`<span offset-key="9990e0003f304a5fa72ec9e1bab61e32:2"> handler using </span>`document.activeElement.click()`<span offset-key="9990e0003f304a5fa72ec9e1bab61e32:4">. </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Document/activeElement" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="23c0822db02b48feb283eb349af40f74" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="4410db61cda74bb0b15cda3867459ef5"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="4410db61cda74bb0b15cda3867459ef5:0">activeElement</code></span></span></a><span key="963dcd7dc00f4ec199f7328d7a3aa772"><span offset-key="963dcd7dc00f4ec199f7328d7a3aa772:0"> which gives us the element that is currently focused on the page.</span></span>

<span key="789cb9ca3cf141499d5d40c0389e11f5"><span offset-key="789cb9ca3cf141499d5d40c0389e11f5:0">This is a lot of extra hassle to build the functionality back in. And there's bound to be other problems with it. </span>**Better to just use the right element for the right job in the first place.**</span>

<span key="04f9fe9e8c3740a4b907fd92cc3ee412">**Meaningful text labels**</span>

<span key="a3a1b7dff0e2439785da4f230bb6ce70"><span offset-key="a3a1b7dff0e2439785da4f230bb6ce70:0">UI control text labels are very useful to all users, but getting them right is particularly important to users with disabilities.</span></span>

<span key="5221b69e2a6d4a108bf1583e3dce4e8c"><span offset-key="5221b69e2a6d4a108bf1583e3dce4e8c:0">You should make sure that your button and link text labels are understandable and distinctive. Don't just use "Click here" for your labels, as screen reader users sometimes get up a list of buttons and form controls. The following screenshot shows our controls being listed by VoiceOver on Mac.</span></span>

<span key="8f6a48e6361c447ba25d67d2bc57c9ad"><span offset-key="8f6a48e6361c447ba25d67d2bc57c9ad:0">Make sure your labels make sense out of context, read on their own, as well as in the context of the paragraph they are in. For example, the following shows an example of good link text:</span></span>

1

<span key="fbe4b27908c4413dbe1821aefd64fd84"><span offset-key="fbe4b27908c4413dbe1821aefd64fd84:0">&lt;p>Whales are really awesome creatures. &lt;a href="whales.html">Find out more about whales&lt;/a>.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="e6fae7a40d3146088c0f041de7c16867"><span offset-key="e6fae7a40d3146088c0f041de7c16867:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="d492442d8c8343ffba36eb9dccbe84dd"><span offset-key="d492442d8c8343ffba36eb9dccbe84dd:0">but this is bad link text:</span></span>

1

<span key="7f747072496b4d009b2186d45164d702"><span offset-key="7f747072496b4d009b2186d45164d702:0">&lt;p>Whales are really awesome creatures. To find more out about whales, &lt;a href="whales.html">click here&lt;/a>.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="c1299b1aa29d49689c2f098f7381e9e5"><span offset-key="c1299b1aa29d49689c2f098f7381e9e5:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="c5662b1588064e2e8b19685be33e224f">**Note:**<span offset-key="c5662b1588064e2e8b19685be33e224f:1"> You can find a lot more about link implementation and best practices in our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Introduction_to_HTML/Creating_hyperlinks" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b47c11b28c9f430dbf444a561fead870" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="78180128a55943999456f6c9a3e1eeed"><span data-offset-key="78180128a55943999456f6c9a3e1eeed:0">Creating hyperlinks</span></span></span></a><span key="6f4d0704fad749599842eb594e845689"><span offset-key="6f4d0704fad749599842eb594e845689:0"> article. You can also see some good and bad examples at </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/good-links.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bb48626d8698486c844f707554350b29" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="20e545a2981342f6a8fc7c0654de6eb6"><span data-offset-key="20e545a2981342f6a8fc7c0654de6eb6:0">good-links.html</span></span></span></a><span key="8808a72377c541b2898d0e0523dc3b4a"><span offset-key="8808a72377c541b2898d0e0523dc3b4a:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/bad-links.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="561d3d5418f34b63af56693e424f328f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="42b78ce256d64163b19f818438295575"><span data-offset-key="42b78ce256d64163b19f818438295575:0">bad-links.html</span></span></span></a><span key="30db9e056a0d4f28a321dc15f9c46ad4"><span offset-key="30db9e056a0d4f28a321dc15f9c46ad4:0">.</span></span>

<span key="057868ca3c0b42d8b1afc65d117a9b02"><span offset-key="057868ca3c0b42d8b1afc65d117a9b02:0">Form labels are also important for giving you a clue about what you need to enter into each form input. The following seems like a reasonable enough example:</span></span>

1

<span key="6527e7bbd90c4e309ea5ede78c22f0f4"><span offset-key="6527e7bbd90c4e309ea5ede78c22f0f4:0">Fill in your name: &lt;input type="text" id="name" name="name"></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="c219e83a93784b8587cb9146c463f12b"><span offset-key="c219e83a93784b8587cb9146c463f12b:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="e69d9fbb03a7445eb242972522013fad"><span offset-key="e69d9fbb03a7445eb242972522013fad:0">However, this is not so useful for disabled users. There is nothing in the above example to associate the label unambiguously with the form input and make it clear how to fill it in if you cannot see it. If you access this with some screen readers, you may only be given a description along the lines of "edit text."</span></span>

<span key="a9959bf4471846188b9fae3fb776cb13"><span offset-key="a9959bf4471846188b9fae3fb776cb13:0">The following is a much better example:</span></span>

1

<span key="84a8dc810c5e4feba305d1ba10d207eb"><span offset-key="84a8dc810c5e4feba305d1ba10d207eb:0">&lt;div></span></span>

2

<span key="17d76c2ecf644f04831490c5cdac6443"><span offset-key="17d76c2ecf644f04831490c5cdac6443:0"> &lt;label for="name">Fill in your name:&lt;/label></span></span>

3

<span key="4d2b5079552f450a92771d8f1cdfcb4a"><span offset-key="4d2b5079552f450a92771d8f1cdfcb4a:0"> &lt;input type="text" id="name" name="name"></span></span>

4

<span key="a701e23197944f7ab478c936c076bbcb"><span offset-key="a701e23197944f7ab478c936c076bbcb:0">&lt;/div></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="3cbd1923ffc34c33aebff5956f3baf1e"><span offset-key="3cbd1923ffc34c33aebff5956f3baf1e:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="453fa7ddba0a4e498f19af80a72e6d1d"><span offset-key="453fa7ddba0a4e498f19af80a72e6d1d:0">With code like this, the label will be clearly associated with the input; the description will be more like "Fill in your name: edit text."</span></span>

<span key="62f60c37b063479c8859561248048b92"><span offset-key="62f60c37b063479c8859561248048b92:0">As an added bonus, in most browsers associating a label with a form input means that you can click the label to select or activate the form element. This gives the input a bigger hit area, making it easier to select.</span></span>

<span key="8250e7a4328446438a863ca51d3d6e04">**Note:**<span offset-key="8250e7a4328446438a863ca51d3d6e04:1"> you can see some good and bad form examples in </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/good-form.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c48dc4e55b7c45449866525e96a5da77" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3cd9fd916ca04244a1f55e12c4f7d33f"><span data-offset-key="3cd9fd916ca04244a1f55e12c4f7d33f:0">good-form.html</span></span></span></a><span key="48f4fecb3f074e71a48990e3375d72cd"><span offset-key="48f4fecb3f074e71a48990e3375d72cd:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/bad-form.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e7711c4e7414ee0922da9d80dd3bf90" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b86dd5d8394c4839aaa49077aef2dfde"><span data-offset-key="b86dd5d8394c4839aaa49077aef2dfde:0">bad-form.html</span></span></span></a><span key="6fe0c4b09158449f9eab8ef07846fa31"><span offset-key="6fe0c4b09158449f9eab8ef07846fa31:0">.</span></span>

<span key="bd15be846c754680ba91e23f84b1ab21"><span offset-key="bd15be846c754680ba91e23f84b1ab21:0">You can find a nice explanation of the importance of proper text labels, and how to investigate text label issues using the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Tools/Accessibility_inspector" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e710f5e5e624b0e80cd7860c173a267" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="2dda3c489b4949008a40f5606af03adb"><span data-offset-key="2dda3c489b4949008a40f5606af03adb:0">Firefox Accessibility Inspector</span></span></span></a><span key="83f35a5951f24fc99980066bf2f4f93a"><span offset-key="83f35a5951f24fc99980066bf2f4f93a:0">, in the following video:</span></span>

<span key="8778b23158df4fa1a6457ac10b984431"><span offset-key="8778b23158df4fa1a6457ac10b984431:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#accessible_data_tables" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0207463dacf64752a1550bb968a5fd48" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7a7e32d302bd4bdb89ea93dde08e5d81"><span data-offset-key="7a7e32d302bd4bdb89ea93dde08e5d81:0">Accessible data tables</span></span></span></a><span key="3795286bb62c4520a71ae3ecb66e8896"><span offset-key="3795286bb62c4520a71ae3ecb66e8896:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f45436a88cac41a7bf4d529c3a782483"><span offset-key="f45436a88cac41a7bf4d529c3a782483:0">A basic data table can be written with very simple markup, for example:</span></span>

1

<span key="d66446892c0f493e91c1975ca899bff8"><span offset-key="d66446892c0f493e91c1975ca899bff8:0">&lt;table></span></span>

<span key="1e0232394e2d4c9eb8cdd35783632da6"><span offset-key="1e0232394e2d4c9eb8cdd35783632da6:0"> &lt;td>Name&lt;/td></span></span>

<span key="d6758f31af024857a45be6e501c2a0c9"><span offset-key="d6758f31af024857a45be6e501c2a0c9:0"> &lt;td>5&lt;/td></span></span>
