<span key="e8ced092d1ac48979af89c85048e9510"><span offset-key="e8ced092d1ac48979af89c85048e9510:0">&lt;/table></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="7414f79cde00441b9b6ad59c5f2de522"><span offset-key="7414f79cde00441b9b6ad59c5f2de522:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="7f82122e6d7d409ca83bcb732653c6af"><span offset-key="7f82122e6d7d409ca83bcb732653c6af:0">But this has problems â€” there is no way for a screen reader user to associate rows or columns together as groupings of data. To do this, you need to know what the header rows are and if they are heading up rows, columns, etc. This can only be done visually for the above table (see </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/bad-table.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="051f84d990a849b6b664a3dd219d6f51" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f5a68e77503d4f3c9c21e707427b2b0e"><span data-offset-key="f5a68e77503d4f3c9c21e707427b2b0e:0">bad-table.html</span></span></span></a><span key="9ae8be1360cb40be9f9c9f130fe2c813"><span offset-key="9ae8be1360cb40be9f9c9f130fe2c813:0"> and try the example out yourself).</span></span>

<span key="5c7b1cb46f62424c86c102f926e00013"><span offset-key="5c7b1cb46f62424c86c102f926e00013:0">Now have a look at our </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/css/styling-boxes/styling-tables/punk-bands-complete.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ecf885691e16413a8e4638dc104486f7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9b181f0ff8e44cbcaa8c0bb741727db3"><span data-offset-key="9b181f0ff8e44cbcaa8c0bb741727db3:0">punk bands table example</span></span></span></a><span key="61c6276fc3a3485db5ae318c2b7d779d"><span offset-key="61c6276fc3a3485db5ae318c2b7d779d:0"> â€” you can see a few accessibility aids at work here:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="2f8c5f75c8754bdd882259ccb023411a"><span offset-key="2f8c5f75c8754bdd882259ccb023411a:0">Table headers are defined using </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/th" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c4b1859d63b348b381d81e6779691656" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="289e3067bdc24e9f92df6700064e716a"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="289e3067bdc24e9f92df6700064e716a:0">&lt;th&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="7deb623bea74466aac9da18c1b92ed24"><span offset-key="7deb623bea74466aac9da18c1b92ed24:0"> elements â€” you can also specify if they are headers for rows or columns using the </span>`scope`<span offset-key="7deb623bea74466aac9da18c1b92ed24:2"> attribute. This gives you complete groups of data that can be consumed by screen readers as single units.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="df2b2598427a4430a83572f4e30c829b"><span offset-key="df2b2598427a4430a83572f4e30c829b:0">The </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/caption" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="436286e57dfd4e6ba5c1fbfade1dd8bd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b78b1af0a75a4dafb89fbb0cc6e5fddf"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="b78b1af0a75a4dafb89fbb0cc6e5fddf:0">&lt;caption&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="89bd08700bbc4239aba88bf32047a5b5"><span offset-key="89bd08700bbc4239aba88bf32047a5b5:0"> element and </span>`<table>`<span offset-key="89bd08700bbc4239aba88bf32047a5b5:2"> </span>`summary`<span offset-key="89bd08700bbc4239aba88bf32047a5b5:4"> attribute both do similar jobs â€” they act as alt text for a table, giving a screen reader user a useful quick summary of the table's contents. The </span>`<caption>`<span offset-key="89bd08700bbc4239aba88bf32047a5b5:6"> element is generally preferred as it makes it's content accessible to sighted users too, who might also find it useful. You don't really need both.</span></span>

<span key="0c3ccf0950b7496894c6de61bd005c3b">**Note:**<span offset-key="0c3ccf0950b7496894c6de61bd005c3b:1"> See our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Tables/Advanced" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1fa716915920431390c315f27e2bfcae" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c8b12e2f958e4f1ab55df06eff660da8"><span data-offset-key="c8b12e2f958e4f1ab55df06eff660da8:0">HTML table advanced features and accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="c7d2f787639a4480a4ee02f300465327"><span offset-key="c7d2f787639a4480a4ee02f300465327:0"> article for more details about accessible data tables.</span></span>

## 

<span key="624abe640b9e43d190ff9ecb4f66239d"><span offset-key="624abe640b9e43d190ff9ecb4f66239d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#text_alternatives" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f00b1580d3e44cbabd0847202aec7d4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="90f9801ad0ee406c83831ac169f9ede2"><span data-offset-key="90f9801ad0ee406c83831ac169f9ede2:0">Text alternatives</span></span></span></a><span key="7645ccb9aa8947cfb8ae01c0e060d63d"><span offset-key="7645ccb9aa8947cfb8ae01c0e060d63d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="bb87c8f609ee429facaf626cca73b58f"><span offset-key="bb87c8f609ee429facaf626cca73b58f:0">Whereas textual content is inherently accessible, the same cannot necessarily be said for multimedia content â€” image and video content cannot be seen by visually-impaired people, and audio content cannot be heard by hearing-impaired people. We cover video and audio content in detail in the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/Multimedia" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="930bd429de97422d9dfafa299f5d4b53" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="965db7228f9943b9926585e4d40c701d"><span data-offset-key="965db7228f9943b9926585e4d40c701d:0">Accessible multimedia</span></span></span></a><span key="ba3eb3116a2a46309a1eaa269a850544"><span offset-key="ba3eb3116a2a46309a1eaa269a850544:0">, but for this article we'll look at accessibility for the humble </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/img" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b9c29d0e91074e8f9c3816bb36adab79" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9ea1f2ecb204421691f16492e82f8f86"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="9ea1f2ecb204421691f16492e82f8f86:0">&lt;img&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="f1fec393a35f4856b7d9383e4222463e"><span offset-key="f1fec393a35f4856b7d9383e4222463e:0"> element.</span></span>

<span key="9cb0d2fb7d42435f9b0598286442cee9"><span offset-key="9cb0d2fb7d42435f9b0598286442cee9:0">We have a simple example written up, </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/html/accessible-image.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="91cc98105aaa407b813fc8f2d923e362" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="305f4ac81c38435d833f347734d3541b"><span data-offset-key="305f4ac81c38435d833f347734d3541b:0">accessible-image.html</span></span></span></a><span key="0944a60f083c4be6bf4247d491926fdd"><span offset-key="0944a60f083c4be6bf4247d491926fdd:0">, which features four copies of the same image:</span></span>

1

<span key="4b966cfdf31c44e6b85b3deae359db0f"><span offset-key="4b966cfdf31c44e6b85b3deae359db0f:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png"></span></span>

2

<span key="c5f8a93662474f4590f50026d321bc2a"><span offset-key="c5f8a93662474f4590f50026d321bc2a:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span key="18bb2569c8a843c7a5d74d655ce2bb81"><span offset-key="18bb2569c8a843c7a5d74d655ce2bb81:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png"</span></span>

4

<span key="fb24760c9c794e3eae4454f574b7b58f"><span offset-key="fb24760c9c794e3eae4454f574b7b58f:0"> alt="A red Tyrannosaurus Rex: A two legged dinosaur standing upright like a human, with small arms, and a large head with lots of sharp teeth."></span></span>

5

<span key="3922573bf8bf4ea1a8943ad3eb0979f6"><span offset-key="3922573bf8bf4ea1a8943ad3eb0979f6:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

6

<span key="30fd0045e44d472b8e3eb80c683b1c5f"><span offset-key="30fd0045e44d472b8e3eb80c683b1c5f:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png"</span></span>

7

<span key="d777d6d609304adab17e17b596e4183b"><span offset-key="d777d6d609304adab17e17b596e4183b:0"> alt="A red Tyrannosaurus Rex: A two legged dinosaur standing upright like a human, with small arms, and a large head with lots of sharp teeth."</span></span>

8

<span key="faa84d972c3c407fa1adf595b6403792"><span offset-key="faa84d972c3c407fa1adf595b6403792:0"> title="The Mozilla red dinosaur"></span></span>

9

<span key="59914bf870a54efaac6b5b61aa9ea2b0"><span offset-key="59914bf870a54efaac6b5b61aa9ea2b0:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

10

<span key="47f7a0c725e541fdb9668ac2e5d10f74"><span offset-key="47f7a0c725e541fdb9668ac2e5d10f74:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png" aria-labelledby="dino-label"></span></span>

11

<span key="201b8952a8c64e5fbba9147b683a8373"><span offset-key="201b8952a8c64e5fbba9147b683a8373:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

12

<span key="691f4082876f44e0ad89aa4ed59054fb"><span offset-key="691f4082876f44e0ad89aa4ed59054fb:0">&lt;p id="dino-label">The Mozilla red Tyrannosaurus Rex: A two legged dinosaur standing upright like a human, with small arms, and a large head with lots of sharp teeth.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="f5d4a89e12b84f829c84be0554e2b5e0"><span offset-key="f5d4a89e12b84f829c84be0554e2b5e0:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="7d792282b7aa4f328d11d29cbc4bffb7"><span offset-key="7d792282b7aa4f328d11d29cbc4bffb7:0">The first image, when viewed by a screen reader, doesn't really offer the user much help â€” VoiceOver for example reads out "/dinosaur.png, image". It reads out the filename to try to provide some help. In this example the user will at least know it is a dinosaur of some kind, but often files may be uploaded with machine-generated file names (e.g. from a digital camera) and these file names would likely provide no context to the image's content.</span></span>

<span key="345a058976e94dbe810b126c8c2969c3">**Note:**<span offset-key="345a058976e94dbe810b126c8c2969c3:1"> This is why you should never include text content inside an image â€” screen readers can't access it. There are other disadvantages too â€” you can't select it and copy/paste it. Just don't do it!</span></span>

<span key="f7090f94f06544d49c0048d929af121a"><span offset-key="f7090f94f06544d49c0048d929af121a:0">When a screen reader encounters the second image, it reads out the full alt attribute â€” "A red Tyrannosaurus Rex: A two legged dinosaur standing upright like a human, with small arms, and a large head with lots of sharp teeth.".</span></span>

<span key="aa26aa54759f4e318926f4b48cd74d0b"><span offset-key="aa26aa54759f4e318926f4b48cd74d0b:0">This highlights the importance of not only using meaningful file names in case so-called </span>**alt text**<span offset-key="aa26aa54759f4e318926f4b48cd74d0b:2"> is not available, but also making sure that alt text is provided in </span>`alt`<span offset-key="aa26aa54759f4e318926f4b48cd74d0b:4"> attributes wherever possible. Note that the contents of the </span>`alt`<span offset-key="aa26aa54759f4e318926f4b48cd74d0b:6"> attribute should always provide a direct representation of the image and what it conveys visually. Any personal knowledge or extra description shouldn't be included here, as it is not useful for people who have not come across the image before.</span></span>

<span key="4d7d29d1c5064f248dca8d3cda52eee7"><span offset-key="4d7d29d1c5064f248dca8d3cda52eee7:0">One thing to consider is whether your images have meaning inside your content, or whether they are purely for visual decoration, and thus have no meaning. If they are decorative, it is better to write an empty text as a value for </span>`alt`<span offset-key="4d7d29d1c5064f248dca8d3cda52eee7:2"> attribute (see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#empty_alt_attributes" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="facbfb1c516542d193d886df01059ed0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="59163c0e35444549803374020680fc66"><span data-offset-key="59163c0e35444549803374020680fc66:0">Empty alt attributes</span></span></span></a><span key="332d56785c5e42d9bd9299bae7540e40"><span offset-key="332d56785c5e42d9bd9299bae7540e40:0">) or to just include them in the page as CSS background images.</span></span>

<span key="bf7da8424fdb4558b7bb5f2be9229926">**Note:**<span offset-key="bf7da8424fdb4558b7bb5f2be9229926:1"> Read </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Multimedia_and_embedding/Images_in_HTML" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0cc824617aff45e5b601d34e455de394" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0bf068af6bd745a39e7da87a134c3298"><span data-offset-key="0bf068af6bd745a39e7da87a134c3298:0">Images in HTML</span></span></span></a><span key="5d8741a96deb4154af04add70f5ae490"><span offset-key="5d8741a96deb4154af04add70f5ae490:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Multimedia_and_embedding/Responsive_images" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4aedce0b8c1343de87df8b521f9dd5cb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1575d039735c4ac48d4ffcee7a74d12f"><span data-offset-key="1575d039735c4ac48d4ffcee7a74d12f:0">Responsive images</span></span></span></a><span key="782fd328066f4364be7618dc88d98408"><span offset-key="782fd328066f4364be7618dc88d98408:0"> for a lot more information about image implementation and best practices.</span></span>

<span key="03c75b461f7f46d4a202d81fa1c3c567"><span offset-key="03c75b461f7f46d4a202d81fa1c3c567:0">If you do want to provide extra contextual information, you should put it in the text surrounding the image, or inside a </span>`title`<span offset-key="03c75b461f7f46d4a202d81fa1c3c567:2"> attribute, as shown above. In this case, most screen readers will read out the alt text, the title attribute, and the filename. In addition, browsers display title text as tooltips when moused over.</span></span>

<span key="eaf83b98ef284d198c62068045f6a6a8"><span offset-key="eaf83b98ef284d198c62068045f6a6a8:0">Let's have another quick look at the fourth method:</span></span>

1

<span key="2af2a3c71eb14f4faee585191885c142"><span offset-key="2af2a3c71eb14f4faee585191885c142:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png" aria-labelledby="dino-label"></span></span>

2

<span key="b0f2f63ea47b45408a46472c646869ba"><span offset-key="b0f2f63ea47b45408a46472c646869ba:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span key="34d49f782751455dbd19c1fcb1986e5c"><span offset-key="34d49f782751455dbd19c1fcb1986e5c:0">&lt;p id="dino-label">The Mozilla red Tyrannosaurus ... &lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="0bd7a14a7b8948b4a19071f189aadd19"><span offset-key="0bd7a14a7b8948b4a19071f189aadd19:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a"><span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:0">In this case, we are not using the </span>`alt`<span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:2"> attribute at all â€” instead, we have presented our description of the image as a regular text paragraph, given it an </span>`id`<span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:4">, and then used the </span>`aria-labelledby`<span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:6"> attribute to refer to that </span>`id`<span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:8">, which causes screen readers to use that paragraph as the alt text/label for that image. This is especially useful if you want to use the same text as a label for multiple images â€” something that isn't possible with </span>`alt`<span offset-key="bca84f7ca7a04d07b1c3446acac9f53a:10">.</span></span>

<span key="c710d03d30c047b1a8875f13cc06c78b">**Note:**<span offset-key="c710d03d30c047b1a8875f13cc06c78b:1"> </span>`aria-labelledby`<span offset-key="c710d03d30c047b1a8875f13cc06c78b:3"> is part of the </span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-1.1/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fc07eeb05c5b40779a4e050e693ac995" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="15481610689e46ec987fb723c51cdac2"><span data-offset-key="15481610689e46ec987fb723c51cdac2:0">WAI-ARIA</span></span></span></a><span key="6caaf0a91a9b4ed4aa0d85b2303904f0"><span offset-key="6caaf0a91a9b4ed4aa0d85b2303904f0:0"> spec, which allows developers to add in extra semantics to their markup to improve screen reader accessibility where needed. To find out more about how it works, read our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/WAI-ARIA_basics" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a46d7349685b4d77aa173fb55504958b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="df04057b9b8f47cd895d58ca1689e94b"><span data-offset-key="df04057b9b8f47cd895d58ca1689e94b:0">WAI-ARIA Basics</span></span></span></a><span key="6fe47b386be648bbb8635ce1e4e8e194"><span offset-key="6fe47b386be648bbb8635ce1e4e8e194:0"> article.</span></span>

### 

<span key="48a2d3495c364f89a271f77edcab7c40"><span offset-key="48a2d3495c364f89a271f77edcab7c40:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#other_text_alternative_mechanisms" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ea80ca661ca34094bc6445cae8d71889" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a66f7a8b43c04f3abc453adac10cda6b"><span data-offset-key="a66f7a8b43c04f3abc453adac10cda6b:0">Other text alternative mechanisms</span></span></span></a><span key="4683c41dbab74c52abec6688ae111898"><span offset-key="4683c41dbab74c52abec6688ae111898:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="b6c21813f6eb44eea1fc4b28c35a8f2a"><span offset-key="b6c21813f6eb44eea1fc4b28c35a8f2a:0">Images also have another mechanisms available for providing descriptive text. For example, there is a </span>`longdesc`<span offset-key="b6c21813f6eb44eea1fc4b28c35a8f2a:2"> attribute that is meant to point to a separate web document containing an extended description of the image, for example:</span></span>

1

<span key="9ecb24d17aca4b7d868634b750832cfa"><span offset-key="9ecb24d17aca4b7d868634b750832cfa:0">&lt;img src="dinosaur.png" longdesc="dino-info.html"></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="c528868c917742b49b6468d6c3ed13f2"><span offset-key="c528868c917742b49b6468d6c3ed13f2:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="f0dc8f2ca2d648329245d40eb33b33e6"><span offset-key="f0dc8f2ca2d648329245d40eb33b33e6:0">This sounds like a good idea, especially for infographics like big charts with lots of information on them that could perhaps be represented as an accessible data table instead (see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#accessible_data_tables" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ff120e1f95e94c41a86e6d6a86fa8594" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f6cd7113b1824b9ab07777f509d18f78"><span data-offset-key="f6cd7113b1824b9ab07777f509d18f78:0">Accessible data tables</span></span></span></a><span key="90a42658c65243d3bfe77d0eee00092f"><span offset-key="90a42658c65243d3bfe77d0eee00092f:0">). However, </span>`longdesc`<span offset-key="90a42658c65243d3bfe77d0eee00092f:2"> is not supported consistently by screen readers, and the content is completely inaccessible to non-screen reader users. It is arguably much better to include the long description on the same page as the image, or link to it with a regular link.</span></span>

<span key="5fd85cb488fc48c78e231eebb07cfd37"><span offset-key="5fd85cb488fc48c78e231eebb07cfd37:0">HTML5 includes two new elements â€” </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/figure" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c35875bb0e64117a2e1e7a3f811b2f3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a73a140257c144b58040c59db3483ea3"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="a73a140257c144b58040c59db3483ea3:0">&lt;figure&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="aa01eab8983e4bbf8dfef5e18576b7f5"><span offset-key="aa01eab8983e4bbf8dfef5e18576b7f5:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/figcaption" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e34882acf88644ee8dacb6d9044e634d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3c2db0e105704889876a8b78e14aa637"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3c2db0e105704889876a8b78e14aa637:0">&lt;figcaption&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="e851039833354ad4a75f651967863823"><span offset-key="e851039833354ad4a75f651967863823:0"> â€” which are supposed to associate a figure of some kind (it could be anything, not necessarily an image) with a figure caption:</span></span>

1

<span key="3dca39a078474decab4f08e2dd129ab0"><span offset-key="3dca39a078474decab4f08e2dd129ab0:0">&lt;figure></span></span>

2

<span key="4c2a1842da20463caea82cd881a626d3"><span offset-key="4c2a1842da20463caea82cd881a626d3:0"> &lt;img src="dinosaur.png" alt="The Mozilla Tyrannosaurus"></span></span>

3

<span key="d1ba930e5b554aa0a41d0a8e85d070c6"><span offset-key="d1ba930e5b554aa0a41d0a8e85d070c6:0"> &lt;figcaption>A red Tyrannosaurus Rex: A two legged dinosaur standing upright like a human, with small arms, and a large head with lots of sharp teeth.&lt;/figcaption></span></span>

4

<span key="07088a7eeffe4db5a6380302e5a69586"><span offset-key="07088a7eeffe4db5a6380302e5a69586:0">&lt;/figure></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="4357bddd0c4f468eb6e92323111beafc"><span offset-key="4357bddd0c4f468eb6e92323111beafc:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="e315d937a3a94083b8c526054ba94d49"><span offset-key="e315d937a3a94083b8c526054ba94d49:0">Unfortunately, most screen readers don't seem to associate figure captions with their figures yet. That said, the element structure is useful for CSS styling, plus it provides a way to place a description of the image next to it in the source.</span></span>

### 

<span key="f2b1fa9a021a464f94ab17d887e2d1c8"><span offset-key="f2b1fa9a021a464f94ab17d887e2d1c8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#empty_alt_attributes" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b66e0b82b5ef4adf992406ab46f8eee8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="5b23706a454a4f9393c43b3a68a46e5b"><span data-offset-key="5b23706a454a4f9393c43b3a68a46e5b:0">Empty alt attributes</span></span></span></a><span key="8a1c5f8fbe7e492ab1b2eeb98228852b"><span offset-key="8a1c5f8fbe7e492ab1b2eeb98228852b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

1

<span key="4ed1cc32d70941d6a7a1ec7ad6927f33"><span offset-key="4ed1cc32d70941d6a7a1ec7ad6927f33:0">&lt;h3></span></span>

2

<span key="7dc30a8b947a4e8ca3990ceb87346e24"><span offset-key="7dc30a8b947a4e8ca3990ceb87346e24:0"> &lt;img src="article-icon.png" alt=""></span></span>

3

<span key="5c3776e5638a41c2a02e98680193c340"><span offset-key="5c3776e5638a41c2a02e98680193c340:0"> Tyrannosaurus Rex: the king of the dinosaurs</span></span>

4

<span key="74d0b9d731484ecbb09c3d3dcec01089"><span offset-key="74d0b9d731484ecbb09c3d3dcec01089:0">&lt;/h3></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="aaa18afc47d44aa995ee027b9bd1a83d"><span offset-key="aaa18afc47d44aa995ee027b9bd1a83d:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="4b2150928369484e80d7c57760134c44"><span offset-key="4b2150928369484e80d7c57760134c44:0">There may be times where an image is included in a page's design, but its primary purpose is for visual decoration. You'll notice in the code example above that the image's </span>`alt`<span offset-key="4b2150928369484e80d7c57760134c44:2"> attribute is empty â€” this is to make screen readers recognize the image, but not attempt to describe the image (instead they'd just say "image", or similar).</span></span>

<span key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b"><span offset-key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b:0">The reason to use an empty </span>`alt`<span offset-key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b:2"> instead of not including it is because many screen readers announce the whole image URL if no </span>`alt`<span offset-key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b:4"> is provided. In the above example, the image is acting as a visual decoration to the heading it's associated with. In cases like this, and in cases where an image is only decoration and has no content value, you should include an empty </span>`alt`<span offset-key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b:6"> in your </span>`img`<span offset-key="9484941ebda4474c84427690c6e4924b:8"> elements. Another alternative is to use the aria </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/ARIA/Roles" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e43e59246e314885a57d3754dc6a4626" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0de5ccff33a148a08a59be1ab37a29e9"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="0de5ccff33a148a08a59be1ab37a29e9:0">role</code></span></span></a><span key="4001fb39f3a6439c84e3826a49d6e338"><span offset-key="4001fb39f3a6439c84e3826a49d6e338:0"> attribute </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/accessibility/ARIA/roles/presentation_role" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1444f019010a4e489d741fdb78d8aefe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="51a8770242024f25af66107e3635332d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="51a8770242024f25af66107e3635332d:0">role="presentation"</code></span></span></a><span key="117636a9047b436e8356755ea008ac14"><span offset-key="117636a9047b436e8356755ea008ac14:0"> as this also stops screen readers from reading out alternative text.</span></span>

<span key="860c5fa23cb9453d8f5c88ec70d503eb">**Note:**<span offset-key="860c5fa23cb9453d8f5c88ec70d503eb:1"> if possible you should use CSS to display images that are only decorative.</span></span>

## 

<span key="c6adf9c99570431ebc9d8845fde9916a"><span offset-key="c6adf9c99570431ebc9d8845fde9916a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#more_on_links" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="48060f1774c24fbeb6a4e5f0c60c514f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7c68fc124fb8442bbbe58975ad42a46d"><span data-offset-key="7c68fc124fb8442bbbe58975ad42a46d:0">More on links</span></span></span></a><span key="5e489d26a4ba43ed8ec537326d27e248"><span offset-key="5e489d26a4ba43ed8ec537326d27e248:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5a1c5af90ea845d6ab523bda0a2457fc"><span offset-key="5a1c5af90ea845d6ab523bda0a2457fc:0">Links ( the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/a" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a0cb19bd7767443d8177eb6ee218a77c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="4a2f2728134e4807b613d8acd62cfd8b"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="4a2f2728134e4807b613d8acd62cfd8b:0">&lt;a&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="0e1bfe52d81e46318e4d18baf881129f"><span offset-key="0e1bfe52d81e46318e4d18baf881129f:0"> element with an </span>`href`<span offset-key="0e1bfe52d81e46318e4d18baf881129f:2"> attribute ), depending on how they are used, can help or harm accessibility. By default, links are accessible in appearance. They can improve accessibility by helping a user quickly navigate to different sections of a document. They can also harm accessibility if their accessible styling is removed or if JavaScript causes them to behave in unexpected ways.</span></span>

### 

<span key="e9c3d1f417584c938a28d9517d1e3217"><span offset-key="e9c3d1f417584c938a28d9517d1e3217:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#link_styling" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="532ffe74d05f4b5e80b8b63ab951d8f2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="34132eeb458840d49f678535e35b8527"><span data-offset-key="34132eeb458840d49f678535e35b8527:0">Link styling</span></span></span></a><span key="814abb7d01d64c929d41999513d505cf"><span offset-key="814abb7d01d64c929d41999513d505cf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="75c674a4bb6b46a3babec4ac71a2293c"><span offset-key="75c674a4bb6b46a3babec4ac71a2293c:0">By default, links are visually different from other text in both color and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/text-decoration" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4686c8accab040d79f1530c509207143" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="95d6f27f3b3c4d41b618e0da72e1ed74"><span data-offset-key="95d6f27f3b3c4d41b618e0da72e1ed74:0">text-decoration</span></span></span></a><span key="ea663337521c41e0abf77eb5760149a7"><span offset-key="ea663337521c41e0abf77eb5760149a7:0">, with links being blue and underlined by default, purple and underlined if visited, and with a </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/:focus" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cc64095c1a8d41fdb8444715fcef11d3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9782673a4b4743d9b2a5a1b3da6f6e8e"><span data-offset-key="9782673a4b4743d9b2a5a1b3da6f6e8e:0">focus-ring</span></span></span></a><span key="6adddec4e0a24500a403488c26b54e0a"><span offset-key="6adddec4e0a24500a403488c26b54e0a:0"> when they receive keyboard focus.</span></span>

<span key="8ca4200c98f34c7183e8b468d529b155"><span offset-key="8ca4200c98f34c7183e8b468d529b155:0">Color should not be used as the sole method of distinguishing links from non-linking content. Link text color, like all text, has to be significantly different from the background color (</span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Understanding_WCAG/Perceivable/Color_contrast" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="40e34494512341bf958b710de915e4cf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="97d79a46114c4fb085da6d4bf020b0ff"><span data-offset-key="97d79a46114c4fb085da6d4bf020b0ff:0">a 4.5:1 contrast</span></span></span></a><span key="f9c19407832d457f86ed31b9fac6a3a6"><span offset-key="f9c19407832d457f86ed31b9fac6a3a6:0">). In addition, links should visually be significantly different from non-linking text. With a minimum contrast requirement of 3:1 between link text and surrounding text and between default, visited, and focus/active states and a 4:5 contrast between all those state colors and the background color.</span></span>

### 

<span key="e53d16bde10c469089bb535cf535bc8e"><span offset-key="e53d16bde10c469089bb535cf535bc8e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#onclick_events" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4800cbb4d845483690e7764953cf1026" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="96efddf5edcb4541806fd2f252d84fa1"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="96efddf5edcb4541806fd2f252d84fa1:0">onclick</code><span data-offset-key="96efddf5edcb4541806fd2f252d84fa1:1"> events</span></span></span></a><span key="905bf8eae26c45da91c53e0e0ddc1104"><span offset-key="905bf8eae26c45da91c53e0e0ddc1104:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4"><span offset-key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4:0">Anchor tags are often abused with the </span>`onclick`<span offset-key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4:2"> event to create pseudo-buttons by setting </span>**href**<span offset-key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4:4"> to </span>`"#"`<span offset-key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4:6"> or </span>`"javascript:void(0)"`<span offset-key="57ab67c882d840dabdfc8b7e1e0ae1e4:8"> to prevent the page from refreshing.</span></span>

<span key="c93beb919ad847f0996df6c65d06b42c"><span offset-key="c93beb919ad847f0996df6c65d06b42c:0">These values cause unexpected behavior when copying or dragging links, opening links in a new tab or window, bookmarking, and when JavaScript is still downloading, errors out, or is disabled. This also conveys incorrect semantics to assistive technologies (e.g., screen readers). In these cases, it is recommended to use a </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/button" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1902c27ac4b3432ebb83cdd866ad4162" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="136f47aae4f54ca19744a3b3adaa5d1e"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="136f47aae4f54ca19744a3b3adaa5d1e:0">&lt;button&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="f863fedda95f40c2b77358f5eccf01ad"><span offset-key="f863fedda95f40c2b77358f5eccf01ad:0"> instead. In general you should only use an anchor for navigation using a proper URL.</span></span>

### 

<span key="1ea5024b3d2e4c40bd990fc1968cf75a"><span offset-key="1ea5024b3d2e4c40bd990fc1968cf75a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#external_links_and_linking_to_non-html_resources" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1d2365ed815c46d1bcba4f8d1e97edb2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="480719ab9d064d2eaddb8e8f1b5dea1c"><span data-offset-key="480719ab9d064d2eaddb8e8f1b5dea1c:0">External links and linking to non-HTML resources</span></span></span></a><span key="51275fbd38384c898f4ddda6cb83c13e"><span offset-key="51275fbd38384c898f4ddda6cb83c13e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="18487fb58cb3427f9db1cb4f2f69ab52"><span offset-key="18487fb58cb3427f9db1cb4f2f69ab52:0">Links that open in a new tab or window via the </span>`target="_blank"`<span offset-key="18487fb58cb3427f9db1cb4f2f69ab52:2"> declaration and links to whose </span>`href`<span offset-key="18487fb58cb3427f9db1cb4f2f69ab52:4"> value points to a file resource should include an indicator about the behavior that will occur when the link is activated.</span></span>

<span key="9d219478645240a681c66818d264e51f"><span offset-key="9d219478645240a681c66818d264e51f:0">People experiencing low vision conditions, who are navigating with the aid of screen reading technology, or who have cognitive concerns may become confused when the new tab, window, or application is opened unexpectedly. Older versions of screen reading software may not even announce the behavior.</span></span>

<span key="8c50a4ab99a74ff09b7e3463ff92665a">**Link that opens a new tab or window**</span>

1

<span key="c53401950691465aa8e0b220c46f61d8"><span offset-key="c53401950691465aa8e0b220c46f61d8:0">&lt;a target="\_blank" href="https://www.wikipedia.org/">Wikipedia (opens in a new window)&lt;/a></span></span>

    <span key="2c388f5f35e64748820f1a31513b089f"><span offset-key="2c388f5f35e64748820f1a31513b089f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/techniques/hypertext/hypertext_links" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="775dc77925c04321a28590f45f3e2f8b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="28418e06d21f453191b34400be60fd34"><span data-offset-key="28418e06d21f453191b34400be60fd34:0">WebAIM: Links and Hypertext - Hypertext Links</span></span></span></a><span key="28436ba116c847e9bab57bb2db9dd005"><span offset-key="28436ba116c847e9bab57bb2db9dd005:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

    <span key="fcfd119f9c0247f28eaa89dffc02deb1"><span offset-key="fcfd119f9c0247f28eaa89dffc02deb1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Understanding_WCAG/Understandable#guideline_3.2_%E2%80%94_predictable_make_web_pages_appear_and_operate_in_predictable_ways" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="71bf5866544d4e57b6f4be833e836d18" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="dab5025f984e4f5bb08533dcf4e4e17c"><span data-offset-key="dab5025f984e4f5bb08533dcf4e4e17c:0">MDN Understanding WCAG, Guideline 3.2 explanations</span></span></span></a><span key="7a443570b0b9423baac5f49ac91ca311"><span offset-key="7a443570b0b9423baac5f49ac91ca311:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

    <span key="0f9891b3c50340c4bbd83ca2c69b0bfd"><span offset-key="0f9891b3c50340c4bbd83ca2c69b0bfd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/WCAG20-TECHS/G200.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f9cbdd6aebc645a9aa2c7c5c1c2578e5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="2c3bff3a6ddc46a5a3441f4995b7dcf3"><span data-offset-key="2c3bff3a6ddc46a5a3441f4995b7dcf3:0">G200: Opening new windows and tabs from a link only when necessary | W3C Techniques for WCAG 2.0</span></span></span></a><span key="c3ead707b9894a6b8cf3afc05754658a"><span offset-key="c3ead707b9894a6b8cf3afc05754658a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

    <span key="0a0a7f1a8a7e464996b69f7704b30234"><span offset-key="0a0a7f1a8a7e464996b69f7704b30234:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/WCAG20-TECHS/G201.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="453c7834a5514a199a5297d142f2d8da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="02269902090d4574856a429f15783ba8"><span data-offset-key="02269902090d4574856a429f15783ba8:0">G201: Giving users advanced warning when opening a new window | W3C Techniques for WCAG 2.0</span></span></span></a><span key="6573441d9c454e99889b73dfac858229"><span offset-key="6573441d9c454e99889b73dfac858229:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="a1365b9c42924e2990e187c5fbcd6630"><span offset-key="a1365b9c42924e2990e187c5fbcd6630:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#skip_links" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6ab1670b5a88442eb5c77410612e7c1b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8646d60ee4c54387aed04736226593e4"><span data-offset-key="8646d60ee4c54387aed04736226593e4:0">Skip links</span></span></span></a><span key="904c939de71a493cb19cc6a8818077d6"><span offset-key="904c939de71a493cb19cc6a8818077d6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="21b4c1e134bc48ab9e8035f4473b77cf"><span offset-key="21b4c1e134bc48ab9e8035f4473b77cf:0">A skip link, also known as skipnav, is an </span>`a`<span offset-key="21b4c1e134bc48ab9e8035f4473b77cf:2"> element placed as close as possible to the opening </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/body" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a15a47724eab4c0f8ef675e81f84a304" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c38338a4c823460f9557aea1cf06eef8"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c38338a4c823460f9557aea1cf06eef8:0">&lt;body&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="9e312d1f25bc46c3b2bb71b186139203"><span offset-key="9e312d1f25bc46c3b2bb71b186139203:0"> element that links to the beginning of the page's main content. This link allows people to bypass content repeated throughout multiple pages on a website, such as a website's header and primary navigation.</span></span>

<span key="b10deec9006b4a4c9e8761e6a9928a20"><span offset-key="b10deec9006b4a4c9e8761e6a9928a20:0">Skip links are especially useful for people who navigate with the aid of assistive technology such as switch control, voice command, or mouth sticks/head wands, where the act of moving through repetitive links can be a laborious task.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7e8151ae573a45428716ab7d443505f5"><span offset-key="7e8151ae573a45428716ab7d443505f5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/techniques/skipnav/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ea8d9a94b694097a9a5f7493b35c0d8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cfb15205e712492caa1a490ef4bc0068"><span data-offset-key="cfb15205e712492caa1a490ef4bc0068:0">WebAIM: "Skip Navigation" Links</span></span></span></a><span key="f9f12806970a4c2ab65aa13f2f9e8fbc"><span offset-key="f9f12806970a4c2ab65aa13f2f9e8fbc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="4670b18c7d974aa09016bdb12a962025"><span offset-key="4670b18c7d974aa09016bdb12a962025:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.a11yproject.com/posts/2013-05-11-skip-nav-links/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="438af4d6e9674512aa3a84f922e7d681" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b91f46842ddb4ee198089c0b2492b7b2"><span data-offset-key="b91f46842ddb4ee198089c0b2492b7b2:0">Howâ€“to: Use Skip Navigation links - The A11Y Project</span></span></span></a><span key="1e342c0b52584f0fa082634d06368b80"><span offset-key="1e342c0b52584f0fa082634d06368b80:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7ef057548d7e4f19ab9f27e8c20f155c"><span offset-key="7ef057548d7e4f19ab9f27e8c20f155c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Accessibility/Understanding_WCAG/Operable#guideline_2.4_%e2%80%94_navigable_provide_ways_to_help_users_navigate_find_content_and_determine_where_they_are" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fa1617492571430faa4d61f38907dd42" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="65e4edca5bf54f8a8d3ee71a3b468a31"><span data-offset-key="65e4edca5bf54f8a8d3ee71a3b468a31:0">MDN Understanding WCAG, Guideline 2.4 explanations</span></span></span></a><span key="7c8ba39a631543b98af4688f0b18350f"><span offset-key="7c8ba39a631543b98af4688f0b18350f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="02fb8cc28eee4bf5aacea8ab38965495"><span offset-key="02fb8cc28eee4bf5aacea8ab38965495:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/UNDERSTANDING-WCAG20/navigation-mechanisms-skip.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ad57cdf1481c420eb34d3a22bc7ae154" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="aa623f6310544f6e8ba08d78fb64f378"><span data-offset-key="aa623f6310544f6e8ba08d78fb64f378:0">Understanding Success Criterion 2.4.1 | W3C Understanding WCAG 2.0</span></span></span></a><span key="3203df60ce36451c8b27a9c53257b2f9"><span offset-key="3203df60ce36451c8b27a9c53257b2f9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="34f1fc71cac84a638be323fb4b2efc0f"><span offset-key="34f1fc71cac84a638be323fb4b2efc0f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#proximity" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="416717ab28f3453694c207a35deb1ff8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="4a73d80945d84de4ae7c000f374d6f3f"><span data-offset-key="4a73d80945d84de4ae7c000f374d6f3f:0">Proximity</span></span></span></a><span key="90f5e57896b64bca8a3547446f38fb84"><span offset-key="90f5e57896b64bca8a3547446f38fb84:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="3a8d308cbb6a4b58a5043ed145c4e2ac"><span offset-key="3a8d308cbb6a4b58a5043ed145c4e2ac:0">Large amounts of interactive contentâ€”including anchorsâ€”placed in close visual proximity to each other should have space inserted to separate them. This spacing is beneficial for people who suffer from fine motor control issues and may accidentally activate the wrong interactive content while navigating.</span></span>

<span key="d7766de17a834847a52d27c7a20e6c73"><span offset-key="d7766de17a834847a52d27c7a20e6c73:0">Spacing may be created using CSS properties such as </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/margin" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="52093c7c39b94f8aba407a43f58a9c80" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="328c87105d2b468db04bb9f88bb1018b"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="328c87105d2b468db04bb9f88bb1018b:0">margin</code></span></span></a><span key="b939ef57e7b74b40ae77175813c37e50"><span offset-key="b939ef57e7b74b40ae77175813c37e50:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="03c01e5c14c2460a8c09db1afc0a793d"><span offset-key="03c01e5c14c2460a8c09db1afc0a793d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://axesslab.com/hand-tremors/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8963475b078c40178291b587800bbe87" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3bff4d9f254d4d5a8f3b0923a17b43b2"><span data-offset-key="3bff4d9f254d4d5a8f3b0923a17b43b2:0">Hand tremors and the giant-button-problem - Axess Lab</span></span></span></a><span key="425b77c388374c38bba8dd5ab7820a2c"><span offset-key="425b77c388374c38bba8dd5ab7820a2c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="c2d0b149a3ec428486745fd283553d17"><span offset-key="c2d0b149a3ec428486745fd283553d17:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#test_your_skills!" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="35a242b98030489caccacf87e413ed48" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="858c50b7736147d98b1dd98fa2e86a98"><span data-offset-key="858c50b7736147d98b1dd98fa2e86a98:0">Test your skills!</span></span></span></a><span key="f781264dbbcf4b0f9777981dc8e14bf8"><span offset-key="f781264dbbcf4b0f9777981dc8e14bf8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5438890fca5b4550903f3740df0a4900"><span offset-key="5438890fca5b4550903f3740df0a4900:0">You've reached the end of this article, but can you remember the most important information? See </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/Test_your_skills:_HTML_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c2c96af6f92943d4a49306c2f0f0a200" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0d07befd007b483db0dc7ac0ea1d0373"><span data-offset-key="0d07befd007b483db0dc7ac0ea1d0373:0">Test your skills: HTML Accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="fb52e9c14dc54f6a9d92be90c63bbccb"><span offset-key="fb52e9c14dc54f6a9d92be90c63bbccb:0"> to verify that you've retained this information before you move on.</span></span>

## 

<span key="fd1432df4ef047db8f6e9bc860d7beca"><span offset-key="fd1432df4ef047db8f6e9bc860d7beca:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#summary" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6a1481648e934fd8ba1b57e7e3d56f94" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a966f5f0f09e4e40beb49d2ed371801e"><span data-offset-key="a966f5f0f09e4e40beb49d2ed371801e:0">Summary</span></span></span></a><span key="4a0c28a85b354016b85f3b172e350dae"><span offset-key="4a0c28a85b354016b85f3b172e350dae:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="10dce116d56b4e2293d88e90e58aa39d"><span offset-key="10dce116d56b4e2293d88e90e58aa39d:0">You should now be well-versed in writing accessible HTML for most occasions. Our WAI-ARIA basics article will help to fill gaps in this knowledge, but this article has taken care of the basics. Next up we'll explore CSS and JavaScript, and how accessibility is affected by their good or bad use.</span></span>

## 

<span key="65f727ce73534ac1acefe9a98185eb30"><span offset-key="65f727ce73534ac1acefe9a98185eb30:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#css_and_javascript_are_accessible" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d34fa2ea429040a4823bfe3930715637" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="a32f8f65ff4a4092873acd0827d851b1"><span data-offset-key="a32f8f65ff4a4092873acd0827d851b1:0">CSS and JavaScript are accessible?</span></span></span></a><span key="c0ab65d7cb4f4fb9a98c1fb042dee42e"><span offset-key="c0ab65d7cb4f4fb9a98c1fb042dee42e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="8b181f0cb659478cace7b6b734a69411"><span offset-key="8b181f0cb659478cace7b6b734a69411:0">CSS and JavaScript don't have the same immediate importance for accessibility as HTML, but they are still able to help or damage accessibility, depending on how they are used. To put it another way, it is important that you consider some best practice advice to make sure that your use of CSS and JavaScript doesn't ruin the accessibility of your documents.</span></span>

## 

<span key="ee7541bd2a6a4c8d872fa5d34b7395de"><span offset-key="ee7541bd2a6a4c8d872fa5d34b7395de:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#css" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="964f52ca2ead4a51a7fc4e30844d741e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c126ce771db8451f995a26a7d02157ad"><span data-offset-key="c126ce771db8451f995a26a7d02157ad:0">CSS</span></span></span></a><span key="02eedeac41c340c0a159ab47f7a4d3cb"><span offset-key="02eedeac41c340c0a159ab47f7a4d3cb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="f8578f80409f44078d3e014c796e9fb0"><span offset-key="f8578f80409f44078d3e014c796e9fb0:0">Let's start off by looking at CSS.</span></span>

### 

<span key="8df8f5e531164075a53f5acf4163ed5d"><span offset-key="8df8f5e531164075a53f5acf4163ed5d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#correct_semantics_and_user_expectation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fe8eadd8816d4dce93db0ed17126bd8b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="ce3e576ac38a462b868c34e996d6d85e"><span data-offset-key="ce3e576ac38a462b868c34e996d6d85e:0">Correct semantics and user expectation</span></span></span></a><span key="b21aac63d9d947399efe852b42fac172"><span offset-key="b21aac63d9d947399efe852b42fac172:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="997bc009a0764e84a282f621ba882635"><span offset-key="997bc009a0764e84a282f621ba882635:0">It is possible to use CSS to make any HTML element look like </span>*anything*<span offset-key="997bc009a0764e84a282f621ba882635:2">, but this doesn't mean that you should. As we frequently mentioned in our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba8afd30598d41ada95bcbbeda701a46" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c3547673b88242b3873f8101307ea15c"><span data-offset-key="c3547673b88242b3873f8101307ea15c:0">HTML: A good basis for accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="a961ceba0c394ba599f7b824ab327d89"><span offset-key="a961ceba0c394ba599f7b824ab327d89:0"> article, you should use the appropriate semantic element for the job, whenever possible. If you don't, it can cause confusion and usability issues for everyone, but particularly users with disabilities. Using correct semantics has a lot to do with user expectations â€” elements look and behave in certain ways, according to their functionality, and these common conventions are expected by users.</span></span>

<span key="3f0a143a224a47b4b6ed80bf5e19a91a"><span offset-key="3f0a143a224a47b4b6ed80bf5e19a91a:0">As an example, a screen reader user can't navigate a page via heading elements if the developer hasn't appropriately used heading elements to markup the content. By the same token, a heading loses its visual purpose if you style it so it doesn't look like a heading.</span></span>

<span key="ad8c1d1b376d4e3c869f23114e27464c"><span offset-key="ad8c1d1b376d4e3c869f23114e27464c:0">The rule of thumb is that you can update the styling of a page feature to fit in your design, but don't change it so much that it no longer looks or behaves as expected. The following sections summarize the main HTML features to consider.</span></span>

<span key="c91efdff5b8a4968943efdd44a3149eb">**"Standard" text content structure**</span>

<span key="483059a36b094e70a875ebdd2c1d4434"><span offset-key="483059a36b094e70a875ebdd2c1d4434:0">Headings, paragraphs, lists â€” the core text content of your page:</span></span>

1

<span key="f1fe2a6687064d4682b400d78d2bc6ef"><span offset-key="f1fe2a6687064d4682b400d78d2bc6ef:0">&lt;h1>Heading&lt;/h1></span></span>

2

<span key="1296f22e54d2490ebce3ae7a6127966d"><span offset-key="1296f22e54d2490ebce3ae7a6127966d:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span key="e85df451cb1f4d78b9ff3e198e591c41"><span offset-key="e85df451cb1f4d78b9ff3e198e591c41:0">&lt;p>Paragraph&lt;/p></span></span>

4

<span key="e35da82a6cb04281bc9a996351c5bcdf"><span offset-key="e35da82a6cb04281bc9a996351c5bcdf:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

5

<span key="d81b2641451c4332aa10705f8802b0cf"><span offset-key="d81b2641451c4332aa10705f8802b0cf:0">&lt;ul></span></span>

6

<span key="55891946622041f5ac7d247b1fbcf8d7"><span offset-key="55891946622041f5ac7d247b1fbcf8d7:0"> &lt;li>My list&lt;/li></span></span>

7

<span key="59ffd411fcae45749abe6f0f8f58175b"><span offset-key="59ffd411fcae45749abe6f0f8f58175b:0"> &lt;li>has two items.&lt;/li></span></span>

8

<span key="e6436e0e867c491a97046a2a8a8e9934"><span offset-key="e6436e0e867c491a97046a2a8a8e9934:0">&lt;/ul></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="09eae8c60e4c402f8608748f43d53100"><span offset-key="09eae8c60e4c402f8608748f43d53100:0">Some typical CSS might look like this:</span></span>

1

<span key="35256cf5c10a482ba345aa2a2e0055ab"><span offset-key="35256cf5c10a482ba345aa2a2e0055ab:0">h1 {</span></span>

2

3

<span key="c33fab2e2e8d43b4ba60f53e48afdd10"><span offset-key="c33fab2e2e8d43b4ba60f53e48afdd10:0">}</span></span>

4

<span key="31b6e4549ba44c81a2e0fb6fb9e63c1c"><span offset-key="31b6e4549ba44c81a2e0fb6fb9e63c1c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

5

<span key="7c50b0e5fa2f4167b52241ca7ea9e5bd"><span offset-key="7c50b0e5fa2f4167b52241ca7ea9e5bd:0">p, li {</span></span>

6

<span key="d7d2ae55f3b64ab69974d9cb16da54c5"><span offset-key="d7d2ae55f3b64ab69974d9cb16da54c5:0"> line-height: 1.5;</span></span>

7

<span key="ea15669f3f494ccda5b5707cecfc4b8d"><span offset-key="ea15669f3f494ccda5b5707cecfc4b8d:0"> font-size: 1.6rem;</span></span>

8

<span key="ffbc00108a1e4beb8a9b3ed6127f2e8f"><span offset-key="ffbc00108a1e4beb8a9b3ed6127f2e8f:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="044bf7704f0c46f19c34b64913fe8955"><span offset-key="044bf7704f0c46f19c34b64913fe8955:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="dc4e5e2606e64643bdf6c1e32cd2b39c"><span offset-key="dc4e5e2606e64643bdf6c1e32cd2b39c:0">You should:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="13ba48419ad14e5aaa1ee3f64541af26"><span offset-key="13ba48419ad14e5aaa1ee3f64541af26:0">Select sensible font sizes, line heights, letter spacing, etc. to make your text logical, legible, and comfortable to read.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="1b660230ad2c47b38958afb3a802605d"><span offset-key="1b660230ad2c47b38958afb3a802605d:0">Make sure your headings stand out from your body text, typically big and bold like the default styling. Your lists should look like lists.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="9efe64e7b9c04033b45f261d9c75b9c2"><span offset-key="9efe64e7b9c04033b45f261d9c75b9c2:0">Your text color should contrast well with your background color.</span></span>

<span key="5496be23c9dc45baa3c1dc5836c2bd93"><span offset-key="5496be23c9dc45baa3c1dc5836c2bd93:0">See </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Introduction_to_HTML/HTML_text_fundamentals" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6e32a34d58594adc88416375a4b1e2df" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="e28e980b78b84446b52a99d04433f500"><span data-offset-key="e28e980b78b84446b52a99d04433f500:0">HTML text fundamentals</span></span></span></a><span key="e7afffeeb2054d21a430b5ef66265fad"><span offset-key="e7afffeeb2054d21a430b5ef66265fad:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/CSS/Styling_text" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="28cd6d0de7954f61b3e195e850704b0a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b0ed9d4889ab44c2ac292111f77ae75c"><span data-offset-key="b0ed9d4889ab44c2ac292111f77ae75c:0">Styling text</span></span></span></a><span key="ce875b686e93410991df4d8e75c1fbdc"><span offset-key="ce875b686e93410991df4d8e75c1fbdc:0"> for more information.</span></span>

<span key="bab68b40c6cb498e94ed25ef1e5fbaca">**Emphasised text**</span>

<span key="3b0b257ddced4d53958b48bb4d394cf5"><span offset-key="3b0b257ddced4d53958b48bb4d394cf5:0">Inline markup that confers specific emphasis to the text that it wraps:</span></span>

1

<span key="c818c11ebf3d4829917621f232749511"><span offset-key="c818c11ebf3d4829917621f232749511:0">&lt;p>The water is &lt;em>very hot&lt;/em>.&lt;/p></span></span>

2

<span key="99764e09babb4524ae1709b90f2ce4e2"><span offset-key="99764e09babb4524ae1709b90f2ce4e2:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

3

<span key="10c29d500d6a45909b280cadd71f43d3"><span offset-key="10c29d500d6a45909b280cadd71f43d3:0">&lt;p>Water droplets collecting on surfaces is called &lt;strong>condensation&lt;/strong>.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="258d2de45c154fd4b479381359f38136"><span offset-key="258d2de45c154fd4b479381359f38136:0">You might want to add some simple coloring to your emphasised text:</span></span>

1

<span key="a5a1cde09f354ff2b39e5382265cae6b"><span offset-key="a5a1cde09f354ff2b39e5382265cae6b:0">strong, em {</span></span>

2

<span key="100f7fc0a50d48c7be51823394e3e4ca"><span offset-key="100f7fc0a50d48c7be51823394e3e4ca:0"> color: #a60000;</span></span>

<span key="9c4b26402acc4810bdc4c769072bebaa"><span offset-key="9c4b26402acc4810bdc4c769072bebaa:0">}</span></span>

<span key="bb102dd899654140a7cb2a3efe6d366e"><span offset-key="bb102dd899654140a7cb2a3efe6d366e:0">You will however rarely need to style emphasis elements in any significant way. The standard conventions of bold and italic text are very recognisable, and changing the style can cause confusion. For more on emphasis, see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/HTML/Introduction_to_HTML/HTML_text_fundamentals#emphasis_and_importance" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f849c893c00e4462b6683a297b3ada20" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3ffc0d3a22d54102a95a3674fd82ab7a"><span data-offset-key="3ffc0d3a22d54102a95a3674fd82ab7a:0">Emphasis and importance</span></span></span></a><span key="96bae28846914686a04cc4a9da3ba18a"><span offset-key="96bae28846914686a04cc4a9da3ba18a:0">.</span></span>

<span key="f19bddad6c794355b9974498138c9873">**Abbreviations**</span>

<span key="1b28889d0e35416f98656beb83f4e419"><span offset-key="1b28889d0e35416f98656beb83f4e419:0">An element that allows an abbreviation, acronym, or initialization to be associated with its expansion:</span></span>

1

<span key="4c63f4611b6b4311a77c9fb6611283c2"><span offset-key="4c63f4611b6b4311a77c9fb6611283c2:0">&lt;p>Web content is marked up using &lt;abbr title="Hypertext Markup Language">HTML&lt;/abbr>.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="3d2f105c4c2f427bbbfe8c37f5096223"><span offset-key="3d2f105c4c2f427bbbfe8c37f5096223:0">Again, you might want to style it in some simple way:</span></span>

1

<span key="a05cd79e5d784a938bc93f42a9a755f0"><span offset-key="a05cd79e5d784a938bc93f42a9a755f0:0">abbr {</span></span>

<span key="987659d5082d4355bb0124355a438a7e"><span offset-key="987659d5082d4355bb0124355a438a7e:0">The recognized styling convention for abbreviations is a dotted underline, and it is unwise to significantly deviate from this. <span key="29d36094e2714cf58a3229869e951d40">**Links**</span>

<span key="8cde05bada6d4d1a86345876bda631ed"><span offset-key="8cde05bada6d4d1a86345876bda631ed:0">Hyperlinks â€” the way you get to new places on the web:</span></span>

1

<span key="bbf857e9a4b7467a99c6ca75e051f3b8"><span offset-key="bbf857e9a4b7467a99c6ca75e051f3b8:0">&lt;p>Visit the &lt;a href="https://www.mozilla.org">Mozilla homepage&lt;/a>.&lt;/p></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />
