13

<span key="0c93cd66cbb94c01846dfdd667f9c174"><span offset-key="0c93cd66cbb94c01846dfdd667f9c174:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="80ba3877e30740c18a05b1f1431c7069"><span offset-key="80ba3877e30740c18a05b1f1431c7069:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="1a0d7e91b4d84ff98c644d68e5229291"><span offset-key="1a0d7e91b4d84ff98c644d68e5229291:0">The standard link conventions are underlined and a different color (default: blue) in their standard state, another color variation when the link has previously been visited (default: purple), and yet another color when the link is activated (default: red). In addition, the mouse pointer changes to a pointer icon when links are moused over, and the link receives a highlight when focused (e.g. via tabbing) or activated. The following image shows the highlight in both Firefox (a dotted outline) and Chrome (a blue outline):</span></span>

<span key="fc18e6a628284b3c96b3db8db26e29fc"><span offset-key="fc18e6a628284b3c96b3db8db26e29fc:0">You can be creative with link styles, as long as you keep giving users feedback when they interact with the links. Something should definitely happen when states change, and you shouldn't get rid of the pointer cursor or the outline â€” both are very important accessibility aids for those using keyboard controls.</span></span>

<span key="b9938c717841486cbc56ed8ba087f072">**Form elements**</span>

<span key="0a262725bc784b24a1a8fa49ca6a6212"><span offset-key="0a262725bc784b24a1a8fa49ca6a6212:0">Elements to allow users to input data into websites:</span></span>

1

<span key="7a86fc3a03a14ce7ade54852f9955d5b"><span offset-key="7a86fc3a03a14ce7ade54852f9955d5b:0">&lt;div></span></span>

2

<span key="5cd462cd55f44d25a5a65c7b973dde49"><span offset-key="5cd462cd55f44d25a5a65c7b973dde49:0"> &lt;label for="name">Enter your name&lt;/label></span></span>

3

<span key="be794209b2e64048b6823320bf4fea78"><span offset-key="be794209b2e64048b6823320bf4fea78:0"> &lt;input type="text" id="name" name="name"></span></span>

4

<span key="c23514a0334c4b0da2413435df95938a"><span offset-key="c23514a0334c4b0da2413435df95938a:0">&lt;/div></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="840f72966fb44e5eadaafc8e136f9484"><span offset-key="840f72966fb44e5eadaafc8e136f9484:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="9996bbaa806b4341a30f7b37eefbc348"><span offset-key="9996bbaa806b4341a30f7b37eefbc348:0">You can see some good example CSS in our </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/accessibility/css/form-css.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1d8e8e1212724163853239214c7b5f34" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c278160e94ab444681d7f1fc4d919f27"><span data-offset-key="c278160e94ab444681d7f1fc4d919f27:0">form-css.html</span></span></span></a><span key="94cd66844b8543a4b7a652b4f14f562c"><span offset-key="94cd66844b8543a4b7a652b4f14f562c:0"> example (</span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/css/form-css.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3980b151d13c44bc98755e7674774147" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="54a8db9d05f7462dbca843cf381f6d30"><span data-offset-key="54a8db9d05f7462dbca843cf381f6d30:0">see it live</span></span></span></a><span key="0ec9d8be7c81464c97a4f56bd86ee95e"><span offset-key="0ec9d8be7c81464c97a4f56bd86ee95e:0"> also).</span></span>

<span key="abfafc57bb4346d49cf750c851dffc15"><span offset-key="abfafc57bb4346d49cf750c851dffc15:0">Most of the CSS you'll write for forms will be for sizing the elements, lining up labels and inputs, and getting them looking neat and tidy.</span></span>

<span key="4caeba95325543edb4b0b236a061eba9"><span offset-key="4caeba95325543edb4b0b236a061eba9:0">You shouldn't however deviate too much from the expected visual feedback form elements receive when they are focused, which is basically the same as links (see above). You could style form focus/hover states to make this behavior more consistent across browsers or fit in better with your page design, but don't get rid of it altogether â€” again, people rely on these clues to help them know what is going on.</span></span>

<span key="2c41add41c3d47eb9cc5d0f6fce3ae1d">**Tables**</span>

<span key="0a585934d25b4d838376bb8f1f4d0f08"><span offset-key="0a585934d25b4d838376bb8f1f4d0f08:0">Tables for presenting tabular data.</span></span>

<span key="86b744532c7440299c3a504b5e635c15"><span offset-key="86b744532c7440299c3a504b5e635c15:0">You can see a good, simple example of table HTML and CSS in our </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/accessibility/css/table-css.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a20128768aad46fe9c8e20557e4bc8fb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="31bf7107e2624606826b23a1ba1fd5c6"><span data-offset-key="31bf7107e2624606826b23a1ba1fd5c6:0">table-css.html</span></span></span></a><span key="b14d5aea7de24f07b9d00fd9bc721f63"><span offset-key="b14d5aea7de24f07b9d00fd9bc721f63:0"> example (</span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/css/table-css.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d7ff479508fd4b87b97033dc5ef40a17" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8d48f6460a334fe49127bca76b6f546b"><span data-offset-key="8d48f6460a334fe49127bca76b6f546b:0">see it live also</span></span></span></a><span key="a651ffc66ad9472ebadbc2c025022808"><span offset-key="a651ffc66ad9472ebadbc2c025022808:0">).</span></span>

<span key="41a05b1c06a045369c134cd3d61cc3a3"><span offset-key="41a05b1c06a045369c134cd3d61cc3a3:0">Table CSS generally serves to make the table fit better into your design and look less ugly. It is a good idea to make sure the table headers stand out (normally using bold), and use zebra striping to make different rows easier to parse.</span></span>

### 

<span key="72bc8ee9d97b484a83970f0bb9e16b2c"><span offset-key="72bc8ee9d97b484a83970f0bb9e16b2c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#color_and_color_contrast" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="baeef7f3095c4282adcda950183e0c11" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="87c7aa431b394ffa9063a19e58a2a0b8"><span data-offset-key="87c7aa431b394ffa9063a19e58a2a0b8:0">Color and color contrast</span></span></span></a><span key="e935251c82ad404093bfe657ae65fa72"><span offset-key="e935251c82ad404093bfe657ae65fa72:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="4cd0ff709c674ab18bef4f7fafd6609b"><span offset-key="4cd0ff709c674ab18bef4f7fafd6609b:0">When choosing a color scheme for your website, make sure that the text (foreground) color contrasts well with the background color. Your design might look cool, but it is no good if people with visual impairments like color blindness can't read your content.</span></span>

<span key="6f115b9128c14a0187c2ac632aad388c"><span offset-key="6f115b9128c14a0187c2ac632aad388c:0">There is an easy way to check whether your contrast is large enough to not cause problems. There are a number of contrast checking tools online that you can enter your foreground and background colors into, to check them. For example WebAIM's </span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/resources/contrastchecker/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8189ae35850749249c65000aadac91ea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d7b43cf2a72e408db28aecbf79d856fa"><span data-offset-key="d7b43cf2a72e408db28aecbf79d856fa:0">Color Contrast Checker</span></span></span></a><span key="7599ea79087a4e879537d71ff4e3a89d"><span offset-key="7599ea79087a4e879537d71ff4e3a89d:0"> is simple to use, and provides an explanation of what you need to conform to the WCAG criteria around color contrast.</span></span>

<span key="3dd0a06b6b1a4096a9c3e638916bf3f6">**Note:**<span offset-key="3dd0a06b6b1a4096a9c3e638916bf3f6:1"> A high contrast ratio will also allow anyone using a smartphone or tablet with a glossy screen to better read pages when in a bright environment, such as sunlight.</span></span>

<span key="f643e63137dd4e0f8df67723d17e5af7"><span offset-key="f643e63137dd4e0f8df67723d17e5af7:0">Another tip is to not rely on color alone for signposts/information, as this will be no good for those who can't see the color. Instead of marking required form fields in red, for example, mark them with an asterisk and in red.</span></span>

### 

<span key="a2d53f3c7a3e4101aebd1da8495b6ac9"><span offset-key="a2d53f3c7a3e4101aebd1da8495b6ac9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#hiding_things" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0178e6564f2445c0acb396ab6c270ce5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="61171e5c3e8844a2a8152f4fb074fb3a"><span data-offset-key="61171e5c3e8844a2a8152f4fb074fb3a:0">Hiding things</span></span></span></a><span key="92c63e0d127d423595ea56ea353a7b12"><span offset-key="92c63e0d127d423595ea56ea353a7b12:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="03e05d61710049e89145e1b714fadd62"><span offset-key="03e05d61710049e89145e1b714fadd62:0">There are many instances where a visual design will require that not all content is shown at once. For example, in our </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/css/css-layout/practical-positioning-examples/info-box.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5757cd2b5a0140ed883b07426ffeaf7d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="22a9a8dec38e445280837b1dfd3fdf39"><span data-offset-key="22a9a8dec38e445280837b1dfd3fdf39:0">Tabbed info box example</span></span></span></a><span key="7b075e22f5c84d83b33284a4e7d43215"><span offset-key="7b075e22f5c84d83b33284a4e7d43215:0"> (see </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/css/css-layout/practical-positioning-examples/info-box.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4ec301ae4c3d462cb8c2230d840cefb4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="0594434047774c0d994b6a2fceb2ffa7"><span data-offset-key="0594434047774c0d994b6a2fceb2ffa7:0">source code</span></span></span></a><span key="a14560dac70d4180b1bf7c951fe4c912"><span offset-key="a14560dac70d4180b1bf7c951fe4c912:0">) we have three panels of information, but we are </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/CSS/CSS_layout/Positioning" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="970d7fe07df44a17bf1097f7a9893a28" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="38499e32477e4f9c8cf8bedf1d6c3c44"><span data-offset-key="38499e32477e4f9c8cf8bedf1d6c3c44:0">positioning</span></span></span></a><span key="643aec3d9ffe4bb09df37787ed6b3442"><span offset-key="643aec3d9ffe4bb09df37787ed6b3442:0"> them on top of one another and providing tabs that can be clicked to show each one (it is also keyboard accessible â€” you can alternatively use Tab and Enter/Return to select them).</span></span>

<span key="efd00cc6baf441d59eae863e4d2826d2"><span offset-key="efd00cc6baf441d59eae863e4d2826d2:0">Screen reader users don't care about any of this â€” they are happy with the content as long as the source order makes sense, and they can get to it all. Absolute positioning (as used in this example) is generally seen as one of the best mechanisms of hiding content for visual effect, because it doesn't stop screen readers from getting to it.</span></span>

<span key="9e06fb86066a47a9a1aeafe4747d0310"><span offset-key="9e06fb86066a47a9a1aeafe4747d0310:0">On the other hand, you shouldn't use </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/visibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a3c0bcc43e7044ce874a3726d08cfef9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="076781117a43427f921051382224895d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="076781117a43427f921051382224895d:0">visibility</code></span></span></a><span key="4e4eeabd83a140a0b29d369b3310c439">`:hidden`<span offset-key="4e4eeabd83a140a0b29d369b3310c439:1"> or </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/display" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="582fe97137134a45814ce78dc20be153" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7557aad4e2054940a341a9916f611630"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="7557aad4e2054940a341a9916f611630:0">display</code></span></span></a><span key="87c5970ff8c742c38bd6269b4f8f1831">`:none`<span offset-key="87c5970ff8c742c38bd6269b4f8f1831:1">, because they do hide content from screen readers. Unless of course, there is a good reason why you want this content to be hidden from screen readers.</span></span>

<span key="bb49a31cc9974b36aaebf12b10a7ba75">**Note:**<span offset-key="bb49a31cc9974b36aaebf12b10a7ba75:1"> </span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/techniques/css/invisiblecontent/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fdc03116fe794ec5890cc70ddb7eba5e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="4fa55352fcf0459f92d86e486daab2a8"><span data-offset-key="4fa55352fcf0459f92d86e486daab2a8:0">Invisible Content Just for Screen Reader Users</span></span></span></a><span key="0b2997f4fd3a4ac6826d92777cc79a1b"><span offset-key="0b2997f4fd3a4ac6826d92777cc79a1b:0"> has a lot more useful detail surrounding this topic.</span></span>

### 

<span key="fb5363743d304a8b92ea012b7ea3ddb6"><span offset-key="fb5363743d304a8b92ea012b7ea3ddb6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#accept_that_users_can_override_styles" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="20f6a011f785430a94b94415db7d79bb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d20cfa621ff949b8ad4e7b65178e31a4"><span data-offset-key="d20cfa621ff949b8ad4e7b65178e31a4:0">Accept that users can override styles</span></span></span></a><span key="d4cefacd3261453e9119799fd23dd271"><span offset-key="d4cefacd3261453e9119799fd23dd271:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="5d8f3f7eac564cde8b7ec3abd316601a">**Accept that users can override your styles**</span>

<span key="6d98bc3cc5524777b5e96a92d40c3b9e"><span offset-key="6d98bc3cc5524777b5e96a92d40c3b9e:0">It is possible for users to override your styles with their own custom styles, for example:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="360efaabd7c0469c94d99b3b22dac169"><span offset-key="360efaabd7c0469c94d99b3b22dac169:0">See Sarah Maddox's </span></span><a href="https://www.itsupportguides.com/knowledge-base/computer-accessibility/how-to-use-a-custom-style-sheet-css-with-firefox/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99692e664c224669849b42956cbe18a8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1f96562485de48cfba104c11336fbe49"><span data-offset-key="1f96562485de48cfba104c11336fbe49:0">How to use a custom style sheet (CSS) with Firefox</span></span></span></a><span key="efed766f5a0743908a39f27dda445fa5"><span offset-key="efed766f5a0743908a39f27dda445fa5:0"> for a useful guide covering how to do this manually in Firefox, and </span></span><a href="https://www.itsupportguides.com/knowledge-base/computer-accessibility/how-to-use-a-custom-style-sheet-css-with-internet-explorer/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f2a285aecd043a6901187f5e8be8000" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c4ff11a301aa41aabd547fda57567f10"><span data-offset-key="c4ff11a301aa41aabd547fda57567f10:0">How to use a custom style sheet (CSS) with Internet Explorer</span></span></span></a><span key="41cb29d54bbe44b490db1a90006ba328"><span offset-key="41cb29d54bbe44b490db1a90006ba328:0"> by Adrian Gordon for the equivalent IE instructions.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="004fe2312e71423e82dc249eee71551d"><span offset-key="004fe2312e71423e82dc249eee71551d:0">It is probably easier to do it using an extension, for example the Stylish extension is available for </span></span><a href="https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/addon/stylish/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="741f8bd3b4bf4c6184b1bc29a1e074d7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="70f4a1d5e0ad49f298993af8cbccd929"><span data-offset-key="70f4a1d5e0ad49f298993af8cbccd929:0">Firefox</span></span></span></a><span key="a7899b7e648d4479b44857478b03416f"><span offset-key="a7899b7e648d4479b44857478b03416f:0">, </span></span><a href="https://safari-extensions.apple.com/details/?id=com.sobolev.stylish-5555L95H45" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="df9baf4b04274f61a607326062dfbe23" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="6abca184866a43b4b98f529ada4d3cec"><span data-offset-key="6abca184866a43b4b98f529ada4d3cec:0">Safari</span></span></span></a><span key="eb6689bb30a24b8783eddf376101f138"><span offset-key="eb6689bb30a24b8783eddf376101f138:0">, </span></span><a href="https://addons.opera.com/en/extensions/details/stylish/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="362f8bbabfff4606bc99eefa29bac122" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="29ae28045acd413e96a0853a0ce61783"><span data-offset-key="29ae28045acd413e96a0853a0ce61783:0">Opera</span></span></span></a><span key="2e79f1fbb6ef40949028955c66e73df8"><span offset-key="2e79f1fbb6ef40949028955c66e73df8:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/stylish/fjnbnpbmkenffdnngjfgmeleoegfcffe" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="549aaa194ace4ce9b630eb982aeb608d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="d63cc4df20c34854aa51466476a7d551"><span data-offset-key="d63cc4df20c34854aa51466476a7d551:0">Chrome</span></span></span></a><span key="25fe43389c4943f78728bfb279e7094a"><span offset-key="25fe43389c4943f78728bfb279e7094a:0">.</span></span>

<span key="73f41a12611842ac8aeb16d85a15ba45"><span offset-key="73f41a12611842ac8aeb16d85a15ba45:0">Users might do this for a variety of reasons. A visually impaired user might want to make the text bigger on all websites they visit, or a user with severe color deficiency might want to put all websites in high contrast colors that are easy for them to see. Whatever the need, you should be comfortable with this, and make your designs flexible enough so that such changes will work in your design. As an example, you might want to make sure your main content area can handle bigger text (maybe it will start to scroll to allow it all to be seen), and won't just hide it, or break completely.</span></span>

## 

<span key="1a702daa4ba24290acc86a37404425b8"><span offset-key="1a702daa4ba24290acc86a37404425b8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#javascript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="efa873a0cd434bfa852647095df5ce57" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1b7f2eab325240538ba178b007f90c2b"><span data-offset-key="1b7f2eab325240538ba178b007f90c2b:0">JavaScript</span></span></span></a><span key="1d86bae7bf9849629bb1c1aa59d136a8"><span offset-key="1d86bae7bf9849629bb1c1aa59d136a8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="ac5b9b83f1a2409294705a42a9695b85"><span offset-key="ac5b9b83f1a2409294705a42a9695b85:0">JavaScript can also break accessibility, depending on how it is used.</span></span>

<span key="8941c2a912754fef8cf83fc68dab13bd"><span offset-key="8941c2a912754fef8cf83fc68dab13bd:0">Modern JavaScript is a powerful language, and we can do so much with it these days, from simple content and UI updates to fully-fledged 2D and 3D games. There is no rule that says all content has to be 100% accessible to all people â€” you just need to do what you can, and make your apps as accessible as possible.</span></span>

<span key="c4648389976c440fa92cc1a6abffe4af"><span offset-key="c4648389976c440fa92cc1a6abffe4af:0">Simple content and functionality is arguably easy to make accessible â€” for example text, images, tables, forms and push button that activate functions. As we looked at in our </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="61d32c5cba534afaae07dbaf908e2568" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f7c495bf032a47e2af66e26e3c7656b1"><span data-offset-key="f7c495bf032a47e2af66e26e3c7656b1:0">HTML: A good basis for accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="50908669c08f4affbfae2f5bad96bd5a"><span offset-key="50908669c08f4affbfae2f5bad96bd5a:0"> article, the key considerations are:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="6aa13420f79f46f38baf3d1bd520d4a3"><span offset-key="6aa13420f79f46f38baf3d1bd520d4a3:0">Good semantics: Using the right element for the right job. For example, making sure you use headings and paragraphs, and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/button" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0049c52a3d2b4ea9b5d7743708fa1215" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="428a9872d0b04a7a82dbb6419310e998"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="428a9872d0b04a7a82dbb6419310e998:0">&lt;button&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="20ee29695b774cf297c435a26bea9ff8"><span offset-key="20ee29695b774cf297c435a26bea9ff8:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/a" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e6c9c82493c04a9aacacb5283770ace6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="c6fcd375403b49c59c016b8284769595"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c6fcd375403b49c59c016b8284769595:0">&lt;a&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="0832d7cc9dc74048aa6466b4a795e775"><span offset-key="0832d7cc9dc74048aa6466b4a795e775:0"> elements</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5b2a77d0c1c642b69b6a15f3f9579869"><span offset-key="5b2a77d0c1c642b69b6a15f3f9579869:0">Making sure content is available as text, either directly as text content, good text labels for form elements, or </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#text_alternatives" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="240287daf57846dcb0fbb9eb1ba4d880" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="43d194f255e946cdbe5e282fed6348e6"><span data-offset-key="43d194f255e946cdbe5e282fed6348e6:0">text alternatives</span></span></span></a><span key="3b995e1838b448c49a222ab8d48a2a06"><span offset-key="3b995e1838b448c49a222ab8d48a2a06:0">, e.g. alt text for images.</span></span>

<span key="7300d1679e3b4939b5df2d85613ed42c"><span offset-key="7300d1679e3b4939b5df2d85613ed42c:0">We also looked at an example of how to use JavaScript to build in functionality where it is missing â€” see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#building_keyboard_accessibility_back_in" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="49d4c0a002ec4bc5889c880666ef8e2b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cc7efb5d0c79428d870dfe51ca0207f6"><span data-offset-key="cc7efb5d0c79428d870dfe51ca0207f6:0">Building keyboard accessibility back in</span></span></span></a><span key="92ae8858d88e405ca85f61c81df71969"><span offset-key="92ae8858d88e405ca85f61c81df71969:0">. This is not ideal â€” really you should just use the right element for the right job â€” but it shows that it is possible in situations where for some reason you can't control the markup that is used. Another way to improve accessibility for non-semantic JavaScript-powered widgets is to use WAI-ARIA to provide extra semantics for screen reader users. The next article will also cover this in detail.</span></span>

<span key="4cc3a415b9874042bb287b89e3eda248"><span offset-key="4cc3a415b9874042bb287b89e3eda248:0">Complex functionality like 3D games are not so easy to make accessible â€” a complex 3D game created using </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/WebGL_API" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a74ae93de8b148d0b0a23bc83865b099" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="071553c81e35422c94740450520d8212"><span data-offset-key="071553c81e35422c94740450520d8212:0">WebGL</span></span></span></a><span key="7cd9362e51b54d55934e08ff8a88a384"><span offset-key="7cd9362e51b54d55934e08ff8a88a384:0"> will be rendered on a </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/canvas" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="80078c38b9ad491594e7545c263fc8e1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7209657324fd4e6da06ba88ece040e69"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="7209657324fd4e6da06ba88ece040e69:0">&lt;canvas&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="621a068132684a11b99ab78c73cba376"><span offset-key="621a068132684a11b99ab78c73cba376:0"> element, which has no facility at this time to provide text alternatives or other information for severely visually impaired users to make use of. It is arguable that such a game doesn't really have this group of people as a part of its main target audience, and it would be unreasonable to expect you to make it 100% accessible to blind people, however you could implement </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Games/Techniques/Control_mechanisms/Desktop_with_mouse_and_keyboard" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fc7a9cdbdd784e449af5e968a441119d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="242aa42ce9b248438f23f9ffa5562881"><span data-offset-key="242aa42ce9b248438f23f9ffa5562881:0">keyboard controls</span></span></span></a><span key="2b3f427134f14934b1dbd6c9507eaaaf"><span offset-key="2b3f427134f14934b1dbd6c9507eaaaf:0"> so it is usable by non-mouse users, and make the color scheme contrasting enough to be usable by those with color deficiencies.</span></span>

### 

<span key="0ca33354a32343a0885dc599ffdd24e6"><span offset-key="0ca33354a32343a0885dc599ffdd24e6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#the_problem_with_too_much_javascript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc8a37b6a4b4419fb1a48334bba2bff1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="36a9ae3782344e7d80f74c7c95987169"><span data-offset-key="36a9ae3782344e7d80f74c7c95987169:0">The problem with too much JavaScript</span></span></span></a><span key="4b98d86caa7449aba13b75fd5da16a4e"><span offset-key="4b98d86caa7449aba13b75fd5da16a4e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="78bb4113b63a4bed95ca1b8cdac1af07"><span offset-key="78bb4113b63a4bed95ca1b8cdac1af07:0">The problem often comes when people rely on JavaScript too much. Sometimes you'll see a website where everything has been done with JavaScript â€” the HTML has been generated by JavaScript, the CSS has been generated by JavaScript, etc. This has all kinds of accessibility and other issues associated with it, so it is not advised.</span></span>

<span key="f18f6fa471d14d3187b10d59c81d11f9"><span offset-key="f18f6fa471d14d3187b10d59c81d11f9:0">As well as using the right element for the right job, you should also make sure you are using the right technology for the right job! Think carefully about whether you need that shiny JavaScript-powered 3D information box, or whether plain old text would do. Think carefully about whether you need a complex non-standard form widget, or whether a text input would do. And don't generate all your HTML content using JavaScript if at all possible.</span></span>

### 

<span key="ae6a6eac69a04f208cdbe7b9fd7d6da6"><span offset-key="ae6a6eac69a04f208cdbe7b9fd7d6da6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#keeping_it_unobtrusive" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1f0f43e08b52449cbf1632221b5718fc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="4a59cfea515c4dfbbc6c25e0967bfbe1"><span data-offset-key="4a59cfea515c4dfbbc6c25e0967bfbe1:0">Keeping it unobtrusive</span></span></span></a><span key="eea4937987a1477b98c6008ff4e44a6f"><span offset-key="eea4937987a1477b98c6008ff4e44a6f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="0af93dc5dd7b4530a2525964f5787c73"><span offset-key="0af93dc5dd7b4530a2525964f5787c73:0">You should keep </span>**unobtrusive JavaScript**<span offset-key="0af93dc5dd7b4530a2525964f5787c73:2"> in mind when creating your content. The idea of unobtrusive JavaScript is that it should be used wherever possible to enhance functionality, not build it in entirely â€” basic functions should ideally work without JavaScript, although it is appreciated that this is not always an option. But again, a large part of it is using built-in browser functionality where possible.</span></span>

<span key="7f68fc5c9d5546bca416e51cb74be600"><span offset-key="7f68fc5c9d5546bca416e51cb74be600:0">Good example uses of unobtrusive JavaScript include:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="602c62c715ec4de394684d889459dcd8"><span offset-key="602c62c715ec4de394684d889459dcd8:0">Providing client-side form validation, which alerts users to problems with their form entries quickly, without having to wait for the server to check the data. If it isn't available, the form will still work, but validation might be slower.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5cad2724d17943ef8222ba377e23c212"><span offset-key="5cad2724d17943ef8222ba377e23c212:0">Providing custom controls for HTML5 </span>`<video>`<span offset-key="5cad2724d17943ef8222ba377e23c212:2">s that are accessible to keyboard-only users, along with a direct link to the video that can be used to access it if JavaScript is not available (the default </span>`<video>`<span offset-key="5cad2724d17943ef8222ba377e23c212:4"> browser controls aren't keyboard accessible in most browsers).</span></span>

<span key="75ddfb20ce4945a88ae2edd6882ca437"><span offset-key="75ddfb20ce4945a88ae2edd6882ca437:0">As an example, we've written a quick and dirty client-side form validation example â€” see </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/accessibility/css/form-validation.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="15ca69462c2941fd867c5897e154f41c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="1ebbfa419d6e4c67bbb6662e2c623b14"><span data-offset-key="1ebbfa419d6e4c67bbb6662e2c623b14:0">form-validation.html</span></span></span></a><span key="d2c10f47a6a740fcbce4731bf39cda1a"><span offset-key="d2c10f47a6a740fcbce4731bf39cda1a:0"> (also </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/css/form-validation.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fd5b93c1f37a4411b7b9e06bacabf339" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="9a8d43d0ee73408f99ed86b2410efeb5"><span data-offset-key="9a8d43d0ee73408f99ed86b2410efeb5:0">see the demo live</span></span></span></a><span key="907e9ad124d84557a5b6ae998f2d7871"><span offset-key="907e9ad124d84557a5b6ae998f2d7871:0">). Here you'll see a simple form; when you try to submit the form with one or both fields left empty, the submit fails, and an error message box appears to tell you what is wrong.</span></span>

<span key="69e7ddcdb5bc4f92be94505e677925c2"><span offset-key="69e7ddcdb5bc4f92be94505e677925c2:0">This kind of form validation is unobtrusive â€” you can still use the form absolutely fine without the JavaScript being available, and any sensible form implementation will have server-side validation active as well, because it is too easy for malicious users to bypass client-side validation (for example, by turning JavaScript off in the browser). The client-side validation is still really useful for reporting errors â€” users can know about mistakes they make instantly, rather than having to wait for a round trip to the server and a page reload. This is a definite usability advantage.</span></span>

<span key="7a987647a5d2434397c5df449a1f2c69">**Note:**<span offset-key="7a987647a5d2434397c5df449a1f2c69:1"> Server-side validation has not been implemented in this simple demo.</span></span>

<span key="99c2ca3187c04218a9b3b7cd9ba83541"><span offset-key="99c2ca3187c04218a9b3b7cd9ba83541:0">We've made this form validation pretty accessible too. We've used </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/label" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a84d55d3991d48919a402a96db42f53b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="51a20d776302499f80ebbe3b9d848c34"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="51a20d776302499f80ebbe3b9d848c34:0">&lt;label&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="e6e47c16b7f0423cbf66e84b753cbc34"><span offset-key="e6e47c16b7f0423cbf66e84b753cbc34:0"> elements to make sure the form labels are unambiguously linked to their inputs, so screen readers can read them out alongside:</span></span>

1

<span key="08a9e9dc2fe14cfb90bd8febc0cbf5d0"><span offset-key="08a9e9dc2fe14cfb90bd8febc0cbf5d0:0">&lt;label for="name">Enter your name:&lt;/label></span></span>

2

<span key="28a64eeb677b49ea9b1775991c858670"><span offset-key="28a64eeb677b49ea9b1775991c858670:0">&lt;input type="text" name="name" id="name"></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="fb4c4ddd96c548e1b1e96014a80769eb"><span offset-key="fb4c4ddd96c548e1b1e96014a80769eb:0">We only do the validation when the form is submitted â€” this is so that we don't update the UI too often and potentially confuse screen reader (and possibly other) users:</span></span>

7

<span key="5de87a913c5c4e919307982e12ba355d"><span offset-key="5de87a913c5c4e919307982e12ba355d:0"> if(testItem.input.value === '') {</span></span>

8

<span key="38130f03719648b2887f1c71df7bd80a"><span offset-key="38130f03719648b2887f1c71df7bd80a:0"> errorField.style.left = '360px';</span></span>

<span key="ecad107970204e44825872d6eebd58f6"><span offset-key="ecad107970204e44825872d6eebd58f6:0"> createLink(testItem);</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="194fd5af6dc74145ac279d55ab4ed47e"><span offset-key="194fd5af6dc74145ac279d55ab4ed47e:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="5e757f4bb8944c12b9971caaabe530ee">**Note:**<span offset-key="5e757f4bb8944c12b9971caaabe530ee:1"> In this example, we are hiding and showing the error message box using absolute positioning rather than another method such as visibility or display, because it doesn't interfere with the screen reader being able to read content from it.</span></span>

<span key="eb5911314a4f4859bc9792fade4a6e1f"><span offset-key="eb5911314a4f4859bc9792fade4a6e1f:0">Real form validation would be much more complex than this â€” you'd want to check that the entered name actually looks like a name, the entered age is actually a number and is realistic (e.g. nonnegative and less than 4 digits). Here we've just implemented a simple check that a value has been filled in to each input field (</span>`if(testItem.input.value === '')`<span offset-key="eb5911314a4f4859bc9792fade4a6e1f:2">).</span></span>

<span key="1b421db22fc248d3b4e283fbdad4cd47"><span offset-key="1b421db22fc248d3b4e283fbdad4cd47:0">When the validation has been performed, if the tests pass then the form is submitted. If there are errors (</span>`if(errorList.innerHTML !== '')`<span offset-key="1b421db22fc248d3b4e283fbdad4cd47:2">) then we stop the form submitting (using </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Event/preventDefault" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d34263243b32468dbaefdeb30c2b13b3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3874bd025927488db821c08802edf3c0"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3874bd025927488db821c08802edf3c0:0">preventDefault()</code></span></span></a><span key="c347a7af457345b081173c35f59328fd"><span offset-key="c347a7af457345b081173c35f59328fd:0">), and display any error messages that have been created (see below). This mechanism means that the errors will only be shown if there are errors, which is better for usability.</span></span>

<span key="d3ff3e4659ff4c1ba3f3c14521630a15"><span offset-key="d3ff3e4659ff4c1ba3f3c14521630a15:0">For each input that doesn't have a value filled in when the form is submitted, we create a list item with a link and insert it in the </span>`errorList`<span offset-key="d3ff3e4659ff4c1ba3f3c14521630a15:2">.</span></span>

1

<span key="44cd55aa279942479eb188100931543e"><span offset-key="44cd55aa279942479eb188100931543e:0">function createLink(testItem) {</span></span>

2

<span key="7f4e0f5071cd43d8bbaa44e5ebfc6a56"><span offset-key="7f4e0f5071cd43d8bbaa44e5ebfc6a56:0"> const listItem = document.createElement('li');</span></span>

3

<span key="540a56f825c94488914128fa54058ccb"><span offset-key="540a56f825c94488914128fa54058ccb:0"> const anchor = document.createElement('a');</span></span>

4

<span key="35cad0524fd84808993cc5eeeff0b073"><span offset-key="35cad0524fd84808993cc5eeeff0b073:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

5

<span key="0143a0ed83cd42bc80bf75f3f75c8024"><span offset-key="0143a0ed83cd42bc80bf75f3f75c8024:0"> anchor.textContent = testItem.input.name + ' field is empty: fill in your ' + testItem.input.name + '.';</span></span>

6

<span key="fc4a9ddaa4504dad9fac2001a6955eae"><span offset-key="fc4a9ddaa4504dad9fac2001a6955eae:0"> anchor.href = '#' + testItem.input.name;</span></span>

7

<span key="eb0e9f8f78dc46f6918c7ee4ac62623c"><span offset-key="eb0e9f8f78dc46f6918c7ee4ac62623c:0"> anchor.onclick = function() {</span></span>

8

<span key="66dafbd6335346d394c04104ce436e58"><span offset-key="66dafbd6335346d394c04104ce436e58:0"> testItem.input.focus();</span></span>

9

<span key="4694f5f77a8d4a60ad5d283ad6f64d0f"><span offset-key="4694f5f77a8d4a60ad5d283ad6f64d0f:0"> };</span></span>

10

<span key="3cdad0d52f2b472e9c967372e0d6ec80"><span offset-key="3cdad0d52f2b472e9c967372e0d6ec80:0"> listItem.appendChild(anchor);</span></span>

11

<span key="61ed5d8a44b74fa889835a3645a683aa"><span offset-key="61ed5d8a44b74fa889835a3645a683aa:0"> errorList.appendChild(listItem);</span></span>

12

<span key="aeb2f5a06a8c4ba999e93828b08c928a"><span offset-key="aeb2f5a06a8c4ba999e93828b08c928a:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="66a71eba609148779f9308c686556dec"><span offset-key="66a71eba609148779f9308c686556dec:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="abf1e2817dcb43038a7bc8ba7b945a53"><span offset-key="abf1e2817dcb43038a7bc8ba7b945a53:0">Each link serves a dual purpose â€” it tells you what the error is, plus you can click on it/activate it to jump straight to the input element in question and correct your entry.</span></span>

<span key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b">**Note:**<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:1"> The </span>`focus()`<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:3"> part of this example is a bit tricky. Chrome and Edge (and newer versions of IE) will focus the element when the link is clicked, without needing the </span>`onclick`<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:5">/</span>`focus()`<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:7"> block. Safari will only highlight the form element with the link on its own, so needs the </span>`onclick`<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:9">/</span>`focus()`<span offset-key="9b22de2c9216465a8c93cdfeea32568b:11"> block to actually focus it. Firefox doesn't focus the inputs properly at all in this context, so Firefox users can't take advantage of this at present (although everything else works fine). The Firefox issue should be fixed soon â€” work is being done to give Firefox behavior parity with other browsers (see </span></span><a href="https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=277178" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9ef78ba72e7b41338c6965cc5c23b582" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="b7aded61ac0e4b5b854dc48dbcdba681"><span data-offset-key="b7aded61ac0e4b5b854dc48dbcdba681:0">bug 277178</span></span></span></a><span key="1edc000e21ea4091ba9238579f4f1cf5"><span offset-key="1edc000e21ea4091ba9238579f4f1cf5:0">).</span></span>

<span key="f4659234851640c2910a97afe4f92004"><span offset-key="f4659234851640c2910a97afe4f92004:0">In addition, the </span>`errorField`<span offset-key="f4659234851640c2910a97afe4f92004:2"> is placed at the top of the source order (although it is positioned differently in the UI using CSS), meaning that users can find out exactly what's wrong with their form submissions and get to the input elements in question by going back up to the start of the page.</span></span>

<span key="10d4c07dbe0f462ead5d90a407cde86c"><span offset-key="10d4c07dbe0f462ead5d90a407cde86c:0">As a final note, we have used some WAI-ARIA attributes in our demo to help solve accessibility problems caused by areas of content constantly updating without a page reload (screen readers won't pick this up or alert users to it by default):</span></span>

1

<span key="095a5462a502413da077f6e93a4ab3c8"><span offset-key="095a5462a502413da077f6e93a4ab3c8:0">&lt;div class="errors" role="alert" aria-relevant="all"></span></span>

2

<span key="f89e456977364d6b9016504c9847cecb"><span offset-key="f89e456977364d6b9016504c9847cecb:0"> &lt;ul></span></span>

3

<span key="6e58755147bd4276acbe84627545c0cb"><span offset-key="6e58755147bd4276acbe84627545c0cb:0"> &lt;/ul></span></span>

4

<span key="d7d799769fb944bda2c192df9f4c8f39"><span offset-key="d7d799769fb944bda2c192df9f4c8f39:0">&lt;/div></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="bc4ccd3d6f6c4d79a416236cf9b64c90"><span offset-key="bc4ccd3d6f6c4d79a416236cf9b64c90:0">We will explain these attributes in our next article, which covers </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/WAI-ARIA_basics" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="20656943b7304c039c8b8c70cd7f29db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="72405ec03e684d1d8a645649ec3bab55"><span data-offset-key="72405ec03e684d1d8a645649ec3bab55:0">WAI-ARIA</span></span></span></a><span key="8e53a409819e496ebac993219b0e9144"><span offset-key="8e53a409819e496ebac993219b0e9144:0"> in much more detail.</span></span>

<span key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3">**Note:**<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:1"> Some of you will probably be thinking about that fact that HTML5 forms have built-in validation mechanisms like the </span>`required`<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:3">, </span>`min`<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:5">/</span>`minlength`<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:7">, and </span>`max`<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:9">/</span>`maxlength`<span offset-key="014d00617f74427e86e387fc64c79ef3:11"> attributes (see the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Element/input" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0e95f981f249438d89dea3625e6a7442" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="5dec0c21231042bb8f410ab1ba1f303e"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="5dec0c21231042bb8f410ab1ba1f303e:0">&lt;input&gt;</code></span></span></a><span key="d1033a6ccf844809b4b75959aff45430"><span offset-key="d1033a6ccf844809b4b75959aff45430:0"> element reference for more information). We didn't end up using these in the demo because cross-browser support for them is patchy (for example IE10 and above only).</span></span>

<span key="7a057451dade46519bd22850096ab377">**Note:**<span offset-key="7a057451dade46519bd22850096ab377:1"> WebAIM's </span></span><a href="https://webaim.org/techniques/formvalidation/" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="75030d3c4a7443179015130af1811ffb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="ea95c33d06074b87b577ab84c3273058"><span data-offset-key="ea95c33d06074b87b577ab84c3273058:0">Usable and Accessible Form Validation and Error Recovery</span></span></span></a><span key="165640c50fba4c7480ebbffbb902cc02"><span offset-key="165640c50fba4c7480ebbffbb902cc02:0"> provides some further useful information about accessible form validation.</span></span>

### 

<span key="02e0a7cd3c30443a874aec7be6e82ac1"><span offset-key="02e0a7cd3c30443a874aec7be6e82ac1:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#other_javascript_accessibility_concerns" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="55bbb655cf4b4f509f7e18ca7a69481e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="99067407d74f4c9badfadc0fb07035e4"><span data-offset-key="99067407d74f4c9badfadc0fb07035e4:0">Other JavaScript accessibility concerns</span></span></span></a><span key="627f6d772dc44959a47eeb3eedd991d8"><span offset-key="627f6d772dc44959a47eeb3eedd991d8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="468c0fbc30204071a2a370aa52edfbc2"><span offset-key="468c0fbc30204071a2a370aa52edfbc2:0">There are other things to be aware of when implementing JavaScript and thinking about accessibility. We will add more as we find them.</span></span>

<span key="bcaa74cdddac46dabe523f54588b5612">**mouse-specific events**</span>

<span key="99845565fe0b49489a533ee661bc97c2"><span offset-key="99845565fe0b49489a533ee661bc97c2:0">As you will be aware, most user interactions are implemented in client-side JavaScript using event handlers, which allow us to run functions in response to certain events happening. Some events can have accessibility issues. The main example you'll come across is mouse-specific events like </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/mouseover_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cdbcbf93ed7c487b8c34b0cd38ad65bb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="075a4741b0d74fffb3895616f0af6783"><span data-offset-key="075a4741b0d74fffb3895616f0af6783:0">mouseover</span></span></span></a><span key="7059f9082e4b4260847b1099d8073a90"><span offset-key="7059f9082e4b4260847b1099d8073a90:0">, </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/mouseout_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="15941172c951417c9f93c3aef87e4cfd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="cbc8b9b960b542afa6fab24ad54c1b32"><span data-offset-key="cbc8b9b960b542afa6fab24ad54c1b32:0">mouseout</span></span></span></a><span key="ca3a6860d32e44bf90b68692f685adec"><span offset-key="ca3a6860d32e44bf90b68692f685adec:0">, </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/dblclick_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fd285881e69b4762a6d0a7db97e19a2d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="8be8987774f54f0c9e558d2cb39e814a"><span data-offset-key="8be8987774f54f0c9e558d2cb39e814a:0">dblclick</span></span></span></a><span key="1ded0f0fa41842ad802d7d9fbacbf51c"><span offset-key="1ded0f0fa41842ad802d7d9fbacbf51c:0">, etc. Functionality that runs in response to these events will not be accessible using other mechanisms, like keyboard controls.</span></span>

<span key="2fd74634400d479b857ff2b4aba9287c"><span offset-key="2fd74634400d479b857ff2b4aba9287c:0">To mitigate such problems, you should double up these events with similar events that can be activated by other means (so-called device-independent event handlers) â€” </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/focus_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aec09bd8a2914475ada160e355b86b8c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="21b27a05bee847b38761e1cc07a894da"><span data-offset-key="21b27a05bee847b38761e1cc07a894da:0">focus</span></span></span></a><span key="107b8140b00741a1917a423603856e46"><span offset-key="107b8140b00741a1917a423603856e46:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/blur_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bf4173e59a7d428388ffeffc952f59c2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="3b13d8e9869047e99250fd77fe8dbf76"><span data-offset-key="3b13d8e9869047e99250fd77fe8dbf76:0">blur</span></span></span></a><span key="2c7c36566338405899e079a91c949406"><span offset-key="2c7c36566338405899e079a91c949406:0"> would provide accessibility for keyboard users.</span></span>

<span key="344313d122e04eb3816a98d7990cbd56"><span offset-key="344313d122e04eb3816a98d7990cbd56:0">Let's look at an example that highlights when this could be useful. Maybe we want to provide a thumbnail image that shows a larger version of the image when it is moused over or focused (like you'd see on an e-commerce product catalog.)</span></span>

<span key="393b2f9e31cf47c19e4ac52de5288c61"><span offset-key="393b2f9e31cf47c19e4ac52de5288c61:0">We've made a very simple example, which you can find at </span></span><a href="https://mdn.github.io/learning-area/accessibility/css/mouse-and-keyboard-events.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0e019852ae994c5e9d7b387cff076793" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="7b1e1185cfbd4197aa62fbed40e3eeab"><span data-offset-key="7b1e1185cfbd4197aa62fbed40e3eeab:0">mouse-and-keyboard-events.html</span></span></span></a><span key="f223705e0b2a40ffadc9f56e242bc9f2"><span offset-key="f223705e0b2a40ffadc9f56e242bc9f2:0"> (see also the </span></span><a href="https://github.com/mdn/learning-area/blob/master/accessibility/css/mouse-and-keyboard-events.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dc76921076a548da8ba39609d280516b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="bb0be4f9c8354d6393d8b34da23e07b3"><span data-offset-key="bb0be4f9c8354d6393d8b34da23e07b3:0">source code</span></span></span></a><span key="e7d9cac1b0b34924936765d6be49c7ba"><span offset-key="e7d9cac1b0b34924936765d6be49c7ba:0">). The code features two functions that show and hide the zoomed-in image; these are run by the following lines that set them as event handlers:</span></span>

1

<span key="28ef6dcbd30845b58db74a7ce710e327"><span offset-key="28ef6dcbd30845b58db74a7ce710e327:0">imgThumb.onmouseover = showImg;</span></span>

2

<span key="942f912ef3a744e1b964f3eb2369b590"><span offset-key="942f912ef3a744e1b964f3eb2369b590:0">imgThumb.onmouseout = hideImg;</span></span>

3

<span key="596aca4894d645a1962bece79ea08220"><span offset-key="596aca4894d645a1962bece79ea08220:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">â€‹</span></span></span>

4

<span key="5ebc82954bdb4f909d2e3759654480a5"><span offset-key="5ebc82954bdb4f909d2e3759654480a5:0">imgThumb.onfocus = showImg;</span></span>

5

<span key="7014daaa292a4f7da41b3d00df625284"><span offset-key="7014daaa292a4f7da41b3d00df625284:0">imgThumb.onblur = hideImg;</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMDA3Ml8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="b8163d5dd57840bfb7ea90cc5f20261d"><span offset-key="b8163d5dd57840bfb7ea90cc5f20261d:0">Copy to Clipboard</span></span>

<span key="ed1fba3b513f44868410a7302f8c6a21"><span offset-key="ed1fba3b513f44868410a7302f8c6a21:0">The first two lines run the functions when the mouse pointer hovers over and stops hovering over the thumbnail, respectively. This won't allow us to access the zoomed view by keyboard though â€” to allow that, we've included the last two lines, which run the functions when the image is focused and blurred (when focus stops). This can be done by tabbing over the image, because we've included </span>`tabindex="0"`<span offset-key="ed1fba3b513f44868410a7302f8c6a21:2"> on it.</span></span>

<span key="35647030319a4c8491574dd171152a71"><span offset-key="35647030319a4c8491574dd171152a71:0">The </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Element/click_event" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="431f954614c342bd8d2e682bdbee3f92" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f8f0629f529b4784ae9c918a62726c38"><span data-offset-key="f8f0629f529b4784ae9c918a62726c38:0">click</span></span></span></a><span key="4381e9a32deb45898dc755f65499b4b4"><span offset-key="4381e9a32deb45898dc755f65499b4b4:0"> event is interesting â€” it sounds mouse-dependent, but most browsers will activate </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/GlobalEventHandlers/onclick" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="19e4472b23284a78877066f993c4f5d0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="878b805cee284ff1889282c504327cbc"><span data-offset-key="878b805cee284ff1889282c504327cbc:0">onclick</span></span></span></a><span key="3fdc328468c745e99958f33c1b391b2b"><span offset-key="3fdc328468c745e99958f33c1b391b2b:0"> event handlers after Enter/Return is pressed on a link or form element that has focus, or when such an element is tapped on a touchscreen device. This doesn't work by default however when you allow a non-default-focusable event to have focus using tabindex â€” in such cases you need to detect specifically when that exact key is pressed (see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/HTML#building_keyboard_accessibility_back_in" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="52464544c731489da7fa9c27c9f281b6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="065f0a442cf144659e8c7c2250dfca41"><span data-offset-key="065f0a442cf144659e8c7c2250dfca41:0">Building keyboard accessibility back in</span></span></span></a><span key="f0971bc5e53041d1be4a2796fed9470a"><span offset-key="f0971bc5e53041d1be4a2796fed9470a:0">).</span></span>

## 

<span key="dc8d2df9b6ae47678a7626e7349a7dbc"><span offset-key="dc8d2df9b6ae47678a7626e7349a7dbc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript#test_your_skills!" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc7a883267044a34a0eab035f0066cab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="f7ed2eeecd6d49f4a5b7563fd2cd7baa"><span data-offset-key="f7ed2eeecd6d49f4a5b7563fd2cd7baa:0">Test your skills!</span></span></span></a><span key="674f0be2b9044222b30ae4494b04915f"><span offset-key="674f0be2b9044222b30ae4494b04915f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">â€‹</span></span></span>

<span key="0f5bab78b788474b9c55f0b715847e48"><span offset-key="0f5bab78b788474b9c55f0b715847e48:0">You've reached the end of this article, but can you remember the most important information? You can find some further tests to verify that you've retained this information before you move on â€” see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/Accessibility/CSS_and_JavaScript/Test_your_skills:_CSS_and_JavaScript_accessibility" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1ec80965af7d4203b15abadd686250ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-10068_259-10069-237__"><span data-key="48c956efc9554f7cbe67fef570060d97"><span data-offset-key="48c956efc9554f7cbe67fef570060d97:0">Test your skills: CSS and JavaScript accessibility</span></span></span></a><span key="b337cf3449684adc88c9ba6dcfd7f58a"><span offset-key="b337cf3449684adc88c9ba6dcfd7f58a:0">.</span></span>
